Mr. Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Suffering and Achievements
What should our Unification Church leave behind in history? We should leave behind joy. 
There is one thing I am proud of right now. Recently, the teacher met a member who was already suffering from an incurable disease. As he faced death, I tried to understand what kind of heart he had and told him, 'When it's time to die, you should die.' After that, I looked at his expression, and he was not sad at all, saying, 'People come and go anyway, but the only regret I have is that I could not fulfill my responsibility before the will.' 
What will we leave behind?
Unification Church members are different from people in the world. We have confidence in the world after death, centered on the will, that is, the future, and we directly feel this in our cells. 
Many humans who have passed through this world and countless saints and sages who have come and gone throughout history have devoted their lives to the question of where humans come from and where they go, but they have not found the answer and have left. 
On July 28, 1970 (Tuesday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This speech was given after the funeral of former president Yoo Hyun-won under the title 'The Limits of Life and Death,' but the earlier part could not be organized due to poor recording. The title was added by the editor.
8   Suffering and Achievements
The teacher does not wish to live long in this world. However, there is one thing: when I think that there is no one who can care for the Father with the same heart after I am gone, I feel pity for God. Other than that, there are no regrets. 
The desire to live has no limits. Even if one lives for a million years, there are no limits. This is the same even if you ask a grandmother in her sixties or seventies with gray hair. You all have lived for more than 20 years, but what is the use of living long without a purpose? If it were me, I would live in a way that adds to the nation, and in the historical era, I would live in a way that adds to history. Life is necessary to leave goodness behind, to leave something better behind. One should not live like a parasite that only eats. 
I pray every day while commuting by car. Many people travel by car, but whenever I travel anywhere in Seoul, I always pray, 'Please protect this road.' I go for the new will. If I do not, Satan will block my path. The teacher lives like that. 
You have come to understand how your life path has changed by knowing the Unification Church. Recently, I heard a solemn report from someone who had fallen away from the Unification Church. He said, since this is a path that must be taken anyway, he had no choice but to return and asked if he could be accepted again. 
From the perspective of the will, there are things that cannot be answered here. After having traveled the world and done various things, he returned because there was nowhere else to go. However, it is good that he has returned now, but there will be suffering on the path he takes. There will be difficulties beyond what he found difficult in the past, so how will he overcome that? 
He should think for himself whether he can take responsibility for that. If he can take responsibility, I have the generosity to forgive him even ten times. However, if I forgive him when he cannot take responsibility, it will cause him to commit a double sin. So I could not answer and remained silent. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." When he left, he stood up, but when he goes out and comes back, he cannot do that. 
How one spends their life is the issue.
In the future, when the history of suffering endured by those who have walked this path for a long time is revealed to the world, it will remain in history that some people have gone through certain adversities alongside the teacher's history. They did not live well, dress well, or live in good environments, but when they dressed their sons and daughters in hanbok and baji in a small room, that clothing will become a lamp that illuminates a new path for humanity for thousands of years. That is how it will be. 
I have gone in and out of prison many times, and every time I endured unbearable torture, I thought this: the blood shed by loyal patriots who loved their nation is different from the blood I shed. The blood and sweat I shed are different from the blood and sweat they shed. Since I thought they were different once, they will remain different until the end. Even when enemies whip and beat me, I faced them boldly, saying, 'If you want to hit me, go ahead; I will remember your blows.' The teacher has overcome such life-and-death situations. 
Many loyal patriots have shed blood and sacrificed for their country, but I have suffered for heaven and earth, for the historical era, and for the world. If there is someone who can say, 'I will bear everything with my flesh and die,' then that person's heart, which has thought this way, must be testified in the spirit world. The teacher has continued the thread of restoration history with such conviction. 
I will not perish. It is destined that way. Heaven operates in such a way that I will subdue those who strike me. A day will come when many sovereigns will bow their heads to me. I have come this far with such conviction. This is not a boast. It is a principle. You must understand this. 
Therefore, the question is how one spends their life and for what they die. One might answer, 'When I grow old, I will die,' but that is a mistaken thought. The issue is not when one dies but for what one dies. 
Because he became the president of the association and faced such circumstances today, we think deeply of him and welcome him in the spirit world, but the issue is where he died. How wonderful would it be if the president had walked a path that God could love from start to finish? If he could not do that, we should be able to compensate for his shortcomings by doing what he could not do. We must bear that collective responsibility. That is why even living for a thousand years has no limits. 
The path of faith is the path that resolves and transcends the path of death. When it is time to die, one must be prepared to die. After resolving that, the path that the Unification Church walks is this path. 
Do you love your resurrected life more than your wife who has not been resurrected? Do you love your children more than your future resurrected life? One must enter the realm of resurrection. 
Living the suffering that will come after death while alive is the path of duty. That is indemnity. It is the valley that allows people who are destined to go to hell forever to taste all kinds of hellish lives on earth through their seventy or eighty years of life. The purpose of religion is to pave the way to pass through that valley. You must understand this. 
We must pay the indemnity that our nation must bear.
No matter how much you say you will not die, when the time comes, you will die. Before President Yoo went to the spirit world, many people testified. The teacher also knew to some extent, but everyone must go to the spirit world when the time comes. 
There are different types of people who go to the spirit world. Some go according to their destiny, while others do not. Among those who do not go according to their destiny, some receive punishment and die quickly, while others go to indemnify the sins of their nation or the world. 
If three young people in their thirties, who are prominent in a neighborhood, die, that neighborhood will receive blessings. If three young men, who were expected to be great in a clan, die, that clan will receive blessings. This means that indemnity must be paid. This applies everywhere. The law of cause and effect applies everywhere. 
When God places one being of the value of a thousand people in a central position and allows that person to walk the path of death on behalf of a thousand people, the thousand people will be moved by that person's grace, wish to support that person, and aspire to live like that person, then that nation will enter into the same realm of benefits as that person. People aspire to emulate the thoughts of loyal patriots and sages to enter into that realm of benefits. 
Last year, many people went to the spirit world, and this year, many will go as well. Although I did not say it, the teacher already knows everything. Why is this? Because when one steps up a level, indemnity must be paid. 
Now, there is indemnity that the nation must pay. We must do this in our Unification Church. The teacher should have started from a free position right after liberation, but since he could not, we must unite this country to block the fate of communism. 
In Japan, the communist parties are currently sending students from the Chosen Soren to every classroom to promote the overthrow of the Seonggong Alliance. Seeing this, it is truly a serious issue. As reported in today's newspaper, the Chosen Soren is splitting into two factions. It has reached the stage where the Han Deok-su faction and the Kim Amuga faction are dividing and breaking apart. They were supposed to hold a general assembly this time but could not, and a conflict with us has arisen. They are trying to strike us, but if we just fulfill our responsibilities, God will be with us. 
12   Suffering and Achievements
Each of you must fulfill your mission in this era, so obey the orders. I am directly commanding President Kuboki. Therefore, you must obey the president's orders. The Japanese government is currently opposing us. 
President Kuboki has promised to meet with the CIA head of the Far East region this evening. The teacher instructed that President Kuboki meet with the CIA head of the Far East and the CIA representative in Washington to finalize the world anti-communist conference. If it does not work out, he said to grab them by the neck and weep. 
If the United States is defeated by communists in Asia, heaven and earth will also be defeated. Since President Kuboki is going to meet with the CIA head and Prime Minister Kishi, the U.S. State Department has investigated who Kuboki is. However, the assistant at the U.S. embassy spoke quite positively about President Kuboki. So a message has come to meet. 
There was an article in an American newspaper about a young man in Japan who appeared and claimed that Korea, Japan, and Taiwan should form a military alliance. (The recording briefly cuts out) 
Urgent Ideological Armament of the Entire Nation
In operations for fighting, there are direct operations and indirect operations. If direct operations cannot be carried out, then indirect operations must be done. Indirect operations are encirclement operations. Do you understand what I mean? We are currently in a difficult situation. From the perspective of the will, the withdrawal of U.S. troops from Korea is akin to the withdrawal of heavenly armies. Do you understand? That is the problem. What will the United States use to save us? What do they believe to save us? Do not like the United States. 
I opposed the ceasefire. If I were in Dr. Park's position, I would never have agreed to a ceasefire. No matter what, I would not agree to a ceasefire. Even if there were a ceasefire, I would advocate for a northern expedition. I do not know why Dr. Park made concessions after going so far. He was not supposed to retreat. Even if he did retreat, he should have asked for the restoration of the destruction in South Korea. 
When I met former President Eisenhower directly, I said this: 'The United States has failed in its world policy after World War II.' The first failure was that the policy the U.S. should have pursued immediately after World War II was to finance a global welfare movement centered around religious organizations. If they had invested about 1 billion dollars at that time to create a global welfare fund, the Arab world could not have been communized, and everything would have gone as the teacher said. However, because they did not do this, we must now carry the cross. This is also a problem in Korea. I talked about various issues, including the dismissal of General MacArthur. Therefore, your responsibilities are now important. 
You must not rely on the United States. Do you understand? You are not in a position to rest well, eat well, or sleep well. You must devote your efforts to ideologically arm the nation day and night. 
If 600,000 troops are armed with unification thought, there will be no problem. If that happens, it will not matter what kind of high ground, artillery, or machine guns there are. If we had armed an army of nearly 700,000 with unification thought, would we be afraid of machine guns? It is ridiculous. 
Recently, a certain chief came directly to the training center and said something. After the visit, it is like blowing a trumpet. In the past, they treated us as enemies and drove us away, but now they are asking for help. The head of intelligence has also recently said, 'Oh, please come and evangelize us.' This is someone who used to prevent evangelism. So we believe in God. 
If Kim Il-sung comes out aggressively, we will take him. If he calls tonight, he must go, right? If an order is given, he will go. There is no other way. It will happen within a few hours. With such a strong backing, why should we worry? Because we have established internal and external indemnity conditions that can be guaranteed from that backing, this organization will not collapse. 
14   Suffering and Achievements
That is why the teacher said to sweat and suffer. This suffering is not meant to last for a thousand years.
Even if you live in such difficulty, or even if you live in worse conditions, you must be able to be grateful. Only then can you return the world, right? This is why we do such things. I am not suffering because I have no money. I do not need money. What I always need is the results of hard work. That is why I make you suffer. Whether you are a woman or a man, I send you out in just running shoes and underwear.

If the country collapses, it will be even worse. If you cannot take responsibility, that is what happens. Do you think you will survive? Women, do you think you can walk around in colorful skirts and jackets? If it becomes a communist world, they will catch all the Unification Church members and trample them to death. Living is something you should not even think about. You should try to love that nose, that face, as much as you can. The communists are waiting in front of you with pickaxes and shovels; what will you do?

The time for the Unification Church is approaching, so right now in Japan, the Victory Corps members are engaging in Victory activities, but you are indifferent. Shouldn't you at least be concerned about what is happening? As the waves rise and the typhoon approaches, you should act according to the captain's orders, but you are all doing other things. You think you can survive like that? You cannot survive like that; the Unification Church will absolutely not survive. I cannot lead you if you do not follow. Heaven will not leave it alone and will clean it up completely. That is the reality I am walking on. That is why the Unification Church is frightening. I know this well, which is why I fear my own position as the teacher of the Unification Church.

When the teacher stands before the public, if heaven does not appear before him, he will never stand up. When he tries to speak in front of a large crowd, why would he not have anything to say? He could stand up to promote the Unification Church. However, heaven must first stand in that position for him to stand up.

If he stands up when the time is not right, he will fail. If he strikes the pastors and elders of Korea before the time is right, he will fail. Even people like Elder Park and Elder Na received grace, but both ended up failing, right? Why is that? It is because they did not have the right timing. The teacher knows this, which is why he waits until the time comes. When the time comes, he must stand up. At that time, he must absolutely stand up. Even if he is told not to promote, he must promote even if he has to enter someone else's home. That time will come. Therefore, you must go your way even in this environment.

If you had listened to the teacher, the current situation would not have developed like this. When the teacher told the Japanese members to engage in Victory activities, they said, "What are you talking about in a world that is like a goblin?" They said, "The communists are fighting desperately; how can we talk about anti-communism?" Look at the college campuses these days. They are all filled with communist groups. The demonstration winds are sweeping through the campuses. However, the work is now coming to an end. This is crossing over the hill.

Not long ago, Khrushchev took off his shoe and slammed it on the table while speaking at the UN General Assembly. You all know that, right? Now, the communist faction will decline. They are going to fail. In the end, if they wield their power beyond their authority, they will fail.

The Unification Church has not yet exercised power. Has the Unification Church exercised power? The founder of the Unification Church has only been criticized; have you seen him wielding power? How have other church pastors and elders criticized him? Did they say, "Let's see if you can do it"? (Laughter) They have never said anything like that. Because I know this, I remain quiet.

If I wanted to, I would have confidence in winning that fight with you all. Do you have confidence? "Yes." Do you really have confidence? "Yes." Is that true? "Yes." You say you have confidence because it is just words. If you were to actually do it, your eyes would widen and you would say, "Oh dear." (Laughter) If you do it like that, you will fail.

Words can say they have gone to heaven a hundred times. People who believe in Jesus, pastors, say they have gone to heaven thousands or tens of thousands of times. But when you actually go, what is heaven? It is not heaven; it is hell. You must remember that you should have actions rather than just words. Do you understand?

Soon, the time for the teacher of the Unification Church will come. That time is gradually approaching. The time that is not needed before God will pass. Because that time is approaching, both our family and the association have improved since last year. So the association is surviving, and the local areas are surviving as well.

In this position, you must go out centered on the association. You should not just sing and dance. To meet that time, you must carry out indemnity. In the past, when the Israelite people were leaving Egypt, they painted the blood of the lamb on the doorposts. They devoted themselves to sprinkling the blood throughout the night. You cannot just sleep.

Pray united for the restoration of the nation
We must transcend life and death. To transcend, we must devote ourselves, but do not devote yourselves for yourselves. Do you understand? You must devote yourselves for the nation. In the past, we lived for our families, but that time has passed. Now we must go crazy for the nation. How valuable would it be to go crazy for the nation? If we do that, we can have heaven. The nation includes tribes, and my family is included. Therefore, if you become a loyal subject of the nation, the heart of a filial son in your family will already be established.

So, what will you live for? Will you live for yourselves, or for your wives and children? "I will live for the nation." You are to live for the nation. To say to go for the nation does not mean to go in with a bomb and die.

Since life is something that comes once and goes once, today we should make a new resolution before heaven. Do you understand? "Yes." The more complicated problems come before us, the more you should realize that our time is getting closer. The more difficult the environment becomes, the more you should realize that our time is approaching.

In such times, we must unite with one heart and go before heaven. When the fortune of the world enters a time of bearing fruit in the nation, the heavenly world will be formed. Until that time, we must risk our lives, have confidence, and devote ourselves as we walk this path. When families that fulfill the principles of the heavenly world unite as one, we will shed tears and pray for the nation, and even Satan will bow down. Do you understand? However, if all Unification Church members do not unite, Satan will strike. When the Israelite people went wrong, the foreign nations struck, right? So our Unification Church must unite and pray like that. Men, do you understand? "Yes." Women, do you understand? "Yes."

Earlier, we sang the song of unification, but first, I must unify my body and mind, and then I must unify with the Father. Here, I must go through the process of indemnity, and for that, the unified me must become one centered on my family. Also, if the fortune of heaven has come to the nation, my family must carry out indemnity for the national family.

So, once the national family is established, I must take that family as Abel and obediently go through the seven-year course from the position of Cain. That seven-year course is absolutely necessary. Do you understand? You must go that path. The teacher himself has walked that path. Since the central teacher has walked that path, you must understand how to go that path centered on the teacher's words. Do you understand? "Yes."

Even if your hearts and bodies have become one, you must go through the indemnity course corresponding to the number seven. You must go through the first, second, and third seven-year courses. Even if you cannot directly face God, you must have the determination to meet the day of national liberation centered on the words of the teacher who represents God, and your body and mind must become one to devote yourselves with your lives for seven years in the path of suffering for indemnity. We must walk the path of suffering for the sake of this nation and for the restoration of the world. Those who have gone through all this can stand in the position of Abel from the position of Cain and can participate in the place of glory.

Once the Unification Church grows a little more, the era of tribal liberation will come. In the future, as the Unification Church grows and becomes widely known across the country, the Moon clan will come together saying, "Let's support our teacher, Mr. Moon." Do you understand? On that day, centered on the Moon clan, we will restore many tribes in order.

Once we firmly hold the top, those below will follow. If there is a clan leader, we will connect the tribes all at once centered on that clan leader. If we connect just three tribes, this nation will automatically come over. Do you understand what I mean? If we restore the Kim clan of Gimhae, it will be easy to restore Korea. There are many Kims, many Ys, and then many Parks, right? If we can unite just these few tribes, the restoration of Korea is not a problem.

Also, since I am from the Moon clan, the Moon clan will eventually come with their bags packed and say, "Our clan leader." In the not-so-distant future, that will happen. If we can hold just the top of three or four tribes, it will be simple.

And it is not just tribes; it can also be done centered on religion. There are many sects that are struggling financially and are in a difficult situation. If we can graft those sects and bring them to us, it will be good for everyone—brothers, sisters, fathers, mothers, and the whole neighborhood will be happy, and they will welcome us with open arms. That is only natural. If elsewhere they are paying a salary of 10,000 won, and I offer 20,000 won, they will come dancing with joy. If we do that a few times, they will all come over. It is that simple.

Build results that you can boast about forever
But the problem is, how many people here can manage these people and can boast about them? That is the problem. 

In the past, people were very particular about their genealogy. Even while living with a private door, when they entered their home, they would act like a noble. They would grow mustaches and act like nobles while still talking about their ancestry. What qualifications do they have to boast about their genealogy?

What should genealogy boasting be about? It should be about how our ancestors served the nation with loyalty, and how I, as a descendant of theirs, have served them with the same sincerity as God. Can that be denied?

In the same way, you must have such content. If you do not have that content, your descendants will see you as an unlucky noble. That could happen. However, we have the content to boast about our genealogy. Although we may not know much, we, the members of the Unification Church, have the content to say, "We did this and that on this land."

What is there at the headquarters of the Unification Church? What kind of Unification Church headquarters is this? If you think this building is worth hundreds of millions of won, you should die. However, when you come in here, there is content that allows you to boast about your genealogy. Those who only talk about their genealogy will fail. But if people who love the nation come in, they will all become one.

You cannot endure just by talking about genealogy. Is what we are saying true or false? It is undoubtedly true. Therefore, you must suffer.

You have said that you have suffered until now, but what have you accomplished? What progress have you made since the 1960s? Rather, you have eaten away at it and wasted it. Yet when you talk about having suffered, you say this and that, and it sounds good. It looks like you are eating something like a useless chestnut or a side chestnut, and you worry about what that could mean, but when you put it out there, you still look around and eventually open your eyes wide and speak well. This is what it means to be a noble child. When you stand before the public, you should know how to play the drum and strum the guitar. You have such talents.

What else is different about you compared to worldly people? Rather, it seems like you are rotten and useless. Can you trust just words? You must have results. You must have the content to say, "I have done this." It will not work with just prayer now. If you cannot do it, I will step forward with a sign. If I step forward for just a month, you will accomplish what you could have done in ten years.

If the founder of the Unification Church holds a revival meeting, many people will come. If I do it with the skills I used to have, it will cause a stir. However, I do not step forward because I am doing this to indemnify and restore what this nation opposed. That is why I am doing this now.

Unification Church members must reflect
We have come out while being persecuted by established denominations, yet we have held onto God. Therefore, we have set the condition that we have taken responsibility for what they could not. However, this has also become a problem. We have taken beggars and turned them into nobles, but they are acting like beggars again. This is like taking a chick and raising it, only for it to run back to the mountains. We have raised them to be useful, but they have returned to their old ways. Let’s see how that goes. Will you also become a chick? However, even if you become a chick, I will not fail. In the end, you will be used by the teacher.

Hearing such words may be disappointing, right? The teacher cannot help but use you. I tried to love and raise you like chicks, but if that does not work, what will happen? Even though you are a chick, you were born for your owner. Therefore, if you try to use the Unification Church, you will instead be used by the teacher of the Unification Church.

Look at the teacher of the Unification Church. How does he look? Does he look like someone who will be used by you? (Laughter) Do not even dream of using him. When I first started this path, did I not think about it thousands or tens of thousands of times? I thought about it hundreds of times more than you can imagine. I carefully considered everything and checked, and after confirming it was certain, I started. Do you think I am doing this because your heads are not good enough? Yet you are people whose heads are filled with nothing but paste, and you are walking around as if you are going to fall over on the street. There are many such people. You must understand this.

So, will you become a chick or a rooster? "A rooster." You must become a rooster chick. To do that, you must first pluck out the tail. You must remove the tail of the sinful world. You must paint it red and yellow.

Did you know what religion was from the beginning, what Christianity was, or who Jesus was? You are all hearing this for the first time; you are all just a bunch of rascals. The word "rascal" means "to dry." The word "rascal" means what?
Do you know? It is the ‘fleeing moon’ that is extremely thin. What do you have, you all? You came in for free, so do you have any money or anything? Your eyes are just bright red and round.  
Still, you all run because you joined the Unification Church, but then you stop running because your legs hurt. Isn’t it because you haven’t eaten that your legs hurt? And then you say that the Unification Church is bad and that you can’t stay, and you fall away. I absolutely do not think that way. Will you fall away or not? “I will not fall away.” If you want to fall away, go ahead. Let’s be straightforward about it. (Laughter)  
The founder of the Unification Church, Teacher Moon, will not fail. God is moving together with him. This is definitely a relative relationship. If I put in my sincerity, God will surely be with me. That is a principled matter. The teacher has that confidence and is walking this path.  
Right now, there is a great recession in our country, and during such times, you must pray centered on this nation. There may be people who think that they have done all they need to do and want to take a nap, but is it time to take a nap? Is it time to take a nap? We must go out as one. About ten years ago, it wasn’t like this. But now is a time of racing; can you take a nap? Looking at you all now, it is astonishing.  
You must know that God is present and confront the enemy. We must fight back against the enemy that was expelling us and liberate them. We have entered an era where we can play a significant role in reconciling the group that was chased away and the group that was doing the chasing.  
Establish the dignity of the heavenly warrior  
Teacher Kim Young-woon is also here, but President Nixon signed a check for $3,000 to support the International Federation for Victory Over Communism, which we are active in, in Los Angeles, USA. He also said he would send $100,000. This is how America is helping the activities of the International Federation for Victory Over Communism. This is the actual attitude of a religious person.  
Seeing this, we realize that our time has come to the doorstep. Until now, it has been a time of prayer, but now the day of celebration is approaching. On the day of celebration, it is okay to eat well and take a nap when you are full. But right now, it is a time to struggle and cross that threshold, and you can hear the sounds of preparing for the feast, frying pancakes and making rice cakes; can you sleep? Yet, those who sleep are crazy.  
That is the kind of situation you are in right now. You all, should you run, or what should you do? It is time to run around the neighborhood and spread the news that it is time for a feast. In other words, it is time to evangelize. Yet, when told to go out and evangelize, some people say, “Ah, that season has come again. I should take a break during the vacation.” What can you gain by just resting?  
In the future, you should not envy the children of the gentry. You yourselves are substantial seeds. You must leave a signboard that you are substantial seeds for your descendants. Do not live without a purpose. Do you understand?  
Blessed families,  
Because of these blessed families, I often find myself in trouble. Whenever something happens, it’s always, “Oh, Teacher, what should we do? This family has become like this.” Then what will the teacher do? There are many families, so there are many people with their hands out. It’s just a group fighting to take something from the teacher. Do you have any room to do this or that? You must die if the teacher says die, and you must live if the teacher says live. There is no other way left. Do you feel bad when I say this? Even if you feel bad, it cannot be helped.  
In walking the path of the will, it is the best to just fulfill your responsibilities. There are such cases. Some people thought they were frauds, but after entering the Unification Church, they became real people. Is that possible? Such people remain until the end.  
We have come this far through hardship; can we say we cannot do it now? You must put in more sincerity, shed tears for the nation, and hold your mother and father while crying. <Words> Today, I would like to briefly speak on the topic of "The Turning Point of Good and Evil."

God's Struggles
As you generally know, the world we live in is not a world of goodness. In such a world, aiming for goodness and establishing the purpose of goodness is an extremely difficult task. If the way of life of the people in the world itself is not good, then the society in which those people live is also not good, and if that society is not good, then the nation is also not good. If there are many nations that are not good, we can understand that the world cannot be a good world.

When we think about the historical process that has led to this point, the current era, and the time that may remain in the future, we must understand that establishing the center of goodness in this entire field today and achieving the purpose of goodness is extremely difficult.

When we consider the historical process up to now, countless saints and sages have come and gone. They were greater, more motivated, and stronger than we are today, overcoming all the adversities of their times. They are great and noble figures whose characters cannot be compared to ours, and we know that the path they took in pursuit of goodness was not a smooth one. They pursued a moment of goodness, a place of goodness, often exchanging their lives for death, suffering, and sacrificing their lives.

However, goodness can be seen on a global level, a national level, a ethnic level, a family level, and a personal level. The goodness centered on the individual, the family, the tribe, the nation, and the world must align and move in one direction. However, until now, it has been coming out unilaterally. In other words, it has been developing in different directions: east, west, south, and north.

When we look at people, each of the hundred people is different. Just as each has different ancestors, faces, languages, and behaviors, the direction of goodness that we pursue must also be different. God is working with these people, these forms, and these groups. Therefore, we cannot help but think about how to align the direction of individual goodness with the direction of goodness for the whole purpose.

If God exists, then first, there must be a movement to unify these different directions of goodness into one direction. In this regard, something necessary must emerge to unify them into one direction. Here, God cannot help but think of establishing a horizontal connection centered on a social foundation, transcending nations and ethnicities, to present one direction.

The numerous religions that have appeared in our historical process are intended to provide such a direction. Individuals pursue goodness according to their own conscience. If a person's conscience is oriented toward the east, they pursue goodness centered on the east; if it is toward the west, they pursue goodness centered on the west.

There will be a spring season for individuals, families, nations, and the world. To align the direction of the spring season centered on the global fortune, the global spring season must coincide with the national spring season, and the national spring season must coincide with the ethnic, tribal, family, and individual spring seasons. Without aligning these directions, it is impossible to achieve the purpose of goodness with universality and validity before the whole world. Therefore, the question of how to present a unified direction from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world is a significant issue from God's perspective.

From this viewpoint, it is only natural that there must be a religion that can present one direction. That religion must be able to transcend any specific nation and have an impact on the entire world, regardless of its origins. It must present one direction so that the world can move toward one purpose.

God thinks about how to lead the world toward one purpose, that is, how to present one direction and unify it. Therefore, we can conclude that as the end approaches, the unification of global direction centered on such a religion will inevitably be achieved.

The Relationship Between God and Humanity and the Role of Religion
We can see that God and humanity are in a relationship that cannot be separated. How do we know this? We know it by looking at the human heart. When we look at our hearts, we see that everything that acts within the heart is not something that I command with subjective initiative. My heart itself is always relative. The relative position implies that there is some subject.

It is something that makes our hearts pursue goodness, seek better values, and strive for a better environment of goodness, a force that supports us throughout our lives until we die, but it is not motivated by the self itself. The self is always in a relative position. Conscience operates from a position that is united with a subject.

For example, when we consider plus, there cannot be plus alone; minus must arise. The plus and minus at this time are relative existences to each other. Similarly, your body and mind are also relative existences to each other.

If the body and mind are such relative existences, how did this body not become one? The problem is simple. When the plus mind becomes one, the minus, that is, the body in the relative position, automatically becomes one. However, today, humans do not understand this.

So what does God think about? He thinks about how to create conditions where the body and mind, which are in a current opposing relationship while being originally in a subject-object relationship, can overcome this opposing condition and create conditions where they can mutually need each other based on a common point that humanity universally demands.

Therefore, what does religion pursue? It pursues the heart. So what is the heart? When we look at it centered on the heart itself, when a perfect minus arises, the plus automatically comes into being. You must understand this. Similarly, when a perfect plus arises, a perfect minus automatically arises. This is the principle of heaven and earth.

If today our hearts themselves become a perfect minus, there must be a perfect plus. In other words, if our hearts themselves become a perfect minus, we can seize the perfect plus. The practice of meditation is also aimed at pursuing such a state. That is, it is to reach the world of perfect nothingness through meditation and to start anew from a static state like a horizontal line. That is necessary.

It is also necessary to connect with a new dynamic origin, to touch the pure original foundation of the heart that has not been soiled, and to start from one pulse. It is necessary for that one pulse to become the origin of a new beginning.

36 The Turning Point of Good and Evil
Movement cannot be done alone. To move, there must be a relative existence. There is no way to move without a relative existence. There is no way to act. In this regard, where does the action of conscience come from? It comes from power. Then where does that power come from? That is the question.

What must exist before power? Before there is power, there must be a subject and an object that can establish a relationship. Today, the scientific world says that the universe is made of power and energy. Is that energy the essence of the universe? No. What must exist before that energy? There must be a subject and an object.

Logically, this is an obvious conclusion. For the universe to exist, there must be action, and before that action, there must be power, and before power, there must be a subject and an object.

Then where do the subject and object come from? There must be a foundation from which they can emerge. In our Unification Church, we call this the dual characteristics of the subject and object. This subject and object are not created by humanity itself.

Power itself acts. However, to act, there must be a circuit that can activate that power. Without a way to give and receive, power cannot act. Your heart operates because it has a circulatory system like arteries and veins. In this way, all actions must have a corresponding relationship between subject and object.
What must exist before power? There must be a subject and an object. And for there to be a subject and an object, there must be a foundation. 

So, what comes first? Confusion arises in this world because it cannot distinguish between what comes first and what comes later. What is the subject and what is the object...? All beings in the earthly world we live in today exist in a relationship of subject and object. Just as humans are divided into male and female, all plants and animals are also divided into male and female.

Then, what is the subject? This is currently in a state of confusion. Therefore, it must be turned upside down. When you let go and look, the right hand and the left hand may seem similar at first glance. However, the right hand and the left hand fundamentally differ in direction. Some may not understand this well, but one is on the right side and the other is on the left. Heaven and hell may appear similar, but their directions are different. Ordinary people do not understand this well.

That is why a foundation is needed here. The foundation is what the Unification Church refers to as the essence of reason. Within the essence of reason, there must be the essence of nature and the essence of form.

Since the action of conscience is undoubtedly an action, there must be a subject and an object here. When analyzing the content of that power, there is always a relationship between the subject and the object. The chemical reactions that occur during a chemistry experiment happen in this way. As long as a relative relationship is established, a reaction occurs immediately. This relative relationship and conflicting relationship are the fundamentals of the universe.

So, what is conflict? A plus and a plus are in a conflicting relationship. Centered around such polar opposites and conflicting actions, communists advocate for dialectics.

Is conflict a bad thing? Conflict is essential. Without conflict, circular motion cannot occur. If everything just pulls on each other, it can only be linear, not circular. Even in magnetic fields, plus and minus pull on each other. If they only pull on each other, why does it become circular? It is because of the polar opposites. Plus and plus, minus and minus engage in opposing actions. The closer they are, the more such actions occur, resulting in circular and spherical movements. This is the reaction of direct action.

From this perspective, when you ask if you have a conscience, those who say they do not have one are insane. Even when we think, "I wonder if that person has a heart," it is certain that they have a conscience. Both men and women have a conscience. Regardless of how that conscience appears, every person has a conscience. What does a conscience look like? How does it look? It looks good. It resembles your face. Conscience and face are the inside and outside. The inside and outside are the same.

Since the conscience acts as a power, there must be a subject and an object. What the subject is, I do not know, but when my conscience becomes a complete minus, a complete plus appears immediately. The world of morality is such a world.

Did anyone from the very beginning know that God exists and put in effort? Did you all know whether God exists when you put in effort? However, as you delve deeper into the world of the heart, the range expands more and more. What was initially linear gradually connects laterally, leading to reactions, and just like a radio that produces sound through an antenna, power also comes to you. They say that fire comes to our bodies, right? It is the same principle. Power comes.

How does that power come? It depends on how pure the radio itself is, whether it can cleanly convert the waves coming from a distance or not. So, where is the problem? It lies in us becoming a complete minus. Only by becoming a complete minus can we find a complete plus.

That is why God cannot abandon humanity. If there were no humans, God would also be lonely. Until now, God has been working hard, but as humans struggle and repent for their mistakes, He sometimes becomes disheartened but then comes forth again with new hope. He comes forth with the great hope that in the future, a world of the highest goodness centered around humanity can be achieved. In the process, there is pioneering, innovation, development, and reform. He comes forth while doing this. By doing so, we are moving towards a global spring.

The ideology that can resolve the conflict between body and mind
You are the same. A person with a clear conscience knows whether it will be a good time or a bad time even if they just sit still. There are times when you meet someone for the first time, and they seem like a good person for no reason. What does it mean to seem good for no reason? It means you are drawn to that person. That person is either a complete plus or a high minus. Even if I have a plus character, if they have a higher minus character, I will be drawn to them. And if I am a minus and they are a higher plus, I will also be drawn to them. However, if I am a plus and that person is a stronger plus than me, when we touch, we repel each other.

In our human heart world, there is an action similar to electrical action, an attractive action. This manifests in the form of conscience. You may not be able to distinguish it, but it is the same in your daily life. Everything moves scientifically. Depending on direction and quality, how much and what percentage it merges determines the overall good and bad. Therefore, the action of conscience cannot be independent.

Fundamentally, this is how it is, but the human body and mind are different and always fight. The body must be a minus, and the mind must be a plus, but this has been reversed. In other words, they are in opposition. However, when two negatives repel each other, you can insert a plus, and when two pluses repel each other, you can insert a minus.

The problem is how to insert these into humans who are in conflicting positions. You must seek how to insert a minus if it is a minus, or a plus if it is a plus, into the conflicting positions of body and mind. Presenting the solution to this problem to humanity, which has gone through the history of the struggle between mind and body, is the new ideology. In other words, it is to insert either a plus or a minus into humanity, which is in opposing positions.

This new ideology is a religious thought, but it is a thought about God. It is not a thought about humans but a thought about God. It is not materialism but idealism. It is not human-centered but God-centered. This is the ideology we want to insert.

Therefore, what problems remain for humanity? The problem of how to make 100 percent contact with God remains. Then, how do we make 100 percent contact with God? We must feel God's heart 100 percent, live for God 100 percent, and go to where God wants us to go 100 percent.

How to discern good and evil is the problem
Humanity must be guided to have one purpose, one world, and one direction. However, since there should not be distance between nations, we have connected nations and have established a fourfold nature centered around the east, west, south, and north, bringing together many religious people in between. Now, we are moving forward to present one direction centered around the four major religious cultural spheres. Once this time passes, it will be the end.

However, while it seems like the end is coming, it seems we have arrived at the destination, yet we cannot know what that destination is. This is the problem. In this regard, I realize that the responsibility of our church today is great.

So, what is the problem here? It is how we, at the turning point of good and evil, discern good from evil. Since you have come to the Unification Church, you must discern from here. Just because someone goes to America does not mean they can discern if they cannot do so here.

Then, how do we discern from here? Although we are all Unification Church members, the way to discern good and evil is different for everyone. There are myriad forms. Not everyone is the same. You must understand this. There are eastern types, western types, southern types, and northern types. There are also forms corresponding to the seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter.

When viewed in terms of a day, morning corresponds to spring, daytime corresponds to summer, evening corresponds to autumn, and nighttime corresponds to winter. Similarly, humans have childhood, youth, adulthood, and old age. For humans, the spring season corresponds to adolescence. The summer season corresponds to the 30s, and the autumn season corresponds to around the 40s. After that, one enters the winter season, and when the winter solstice passes, it corresponds to death. 

All principles are like this. Spring, summer, autumn, and winter are like this, and so is a day.

In this way, humans are born according to the laws of heaven and earth. The Book of Changes (I Ching) is in accordance with this principle. Everything is made of yin and yang, and this is referred to as the four images based on whether it is upper-lower yin and yang or left-right yin and yang. From this perspective, people are all different. Jesus also appointed three disciples and established a fourfold nature centered around himself.

In this sense, the four-position foundation we speak of does not contradict the principles of heaven and earth.

Among you, there are people of eastern type, western type, southern type, and northern type. There are also people of spring season, summer season, autumn season, and winter season. There are those who are cold and frozen like ice, and there are those who seem good just to look at. There are those who are always dignified and can extend at any time, which is the character of the summer season. Those who quickly rise and quickly fall are of the autumn season.

In this regard, you must surely align yourselves with one purpose centered on the direction you are in. The problem is how you discern that direction. Therefore, you must first know what type you are. This is especially necessary for young men and women when they marry.

If you look at the spring and summer seasons, the spring season seeks the summer season, but the summer season expels the spring season. One side pushes away while the other side pulls in. Isn’t that right? As one day passes, summer gets closer while spring gets further away. One side pulls while the other side pushes away. This is why a circular path exists; if it cannot form a circle, it will be a permanent separation. That is why the universe operates according to the law of the circle. Thus, spring, summer, autumn, and winter must return. If you draw this on a flat surface, it will form a sine curve.

Discerning good and evil causes conflict
You must first discern whether it is good or evil. Where is good and evil? Good and evil are filled in the world, but the turning point where good and evil must be discerned is within yourselves. You must understand this. When the world is seen as evil, those who live without conflict with that evil world are evil people. Those who say they live without conflict with this world are evil people. Even if they are caught in the net of the fallen world, those who live without raising a rebellion are evil people. When it is time to engage in conflict with the world of evil, those who simply live as they are are evil people. If you know that the world you live in is an evil world, you must raise a rebellion.

So why did it come to this? It is because humanity has fallen. Because humanity has fallen and descended, to achieve liberation, one must rise again, and to rise again, one must struggle. It cannot be done just as it is. Through such people, humanity cannot welcome the new world it seeks, cannot expect the development of new history, and cannot leave traces of historical goodness. That is why those who come forth with goodness must struggle.

Communists claim that struggle is necessary for the development of history. They have brought forth dialectical materialism and the logic of thesis-antithesis-synthesis. Our lives pass by in ten or twenty years without notice. When facing the teacher or God, we must not only look at the external aspects. We must feel the internal love. We must be connected by something that cannot be severed forever. We must feel God's love and longing for God.

Love is unchanging. Whether one goes up or down, falls or drops, it must be unchanging. One must feel the Father’s caress even while sleeping. One must always be in a position that cannot be severed. 

How can one go anywhere after uprooting oneself? One cannot go. Because of that heart, one always longs, so one knows just by a glance. 

What we preach through principles is a movement to find love. The world of heart transcends time and space. Both words and prayers ultimately exist for love. Completion is to achieve the ideal of love.

<Words> We are in a fallen position, but we are seeking a new purpose and a new worldview.
The new meaning does not stem from existing assumptions, whether in the family or in society, nor is it something that can be commonly felt by anyone. It is not bound by circumstances. We are presenting a content that can discern this fallen world, with a clear task placed before us, and we are pursuing something new that does not exist in this world. This must be true for my individual self, for my family, and for any society, nation, or the world, as we seek true individuals, true families, true societies, true nations, and a true world centered around genuine content.

Truth and Love
Truth is not dualistic. Although the direction may differ when viewed from the east, west, south, or north, the essence is a singular form that everyone can universally recognize. Where can we discover this true singular form? We cannot claim our outward appearance or the environmental context we live in as the true form. Truth is eternal and unchanging. It must be an absolute standard that can unify all things as the ultimate truth; otherwise, it cannot be considered truth. So, where can this truth settle? That is the question. The place is beyond the concept of 'self.' Therefore, my body and mind constantly yearn for truth.

Then, where can truth be realized in reality? It cannot be determined by the vast world we often envision. It is also not a place centered around society or family. Since I exist before there is a family, the decisive place where truth settles is 'myself.' So, what will we take as the point of settlement within myself? I cannot help but present the vague proposition of love.

What kind of love should that be? It must be a love that can endure eternally. When we encounter that love, eternal happiness dwells within, and when we establish a relationship with that love, we should be able to transcend any distance and environment, connecting beyond time. Such love is essential. Furthermore, that love must be absolute love. It must be something that no historical era can displace. It should be a love that cannot be displaced by the past, present, or future. Therefore, it cannot be a love that feels limited in its encounter with the immutable itself. It must be an infinite love.

It should be a love that overflows with the essence of spring, a love that can melt the snow and ice during the cold winter season, a love that is immeasurable in height or breadth. Such love must establish a stable center within me, never leaving my side. When that love is infinitely felt and sensed, it is indeed capable of contending with the universe. There is no value in this world that can be found apart from that love. If someone has established the absolute love, which is the same at the beginning and the end, at the core of their being, that person, though an individual, can contend with the world.

However, if someone who has felt and possessed such love loses it, that would be the greatest sorrow among sorrows. There is no sorrow greater than the sorrow of having lost that love. Also, what is the greatest misfortune? It is being in a position where one has lost that love and cannot find it again. We cannot overlook such realities. Therefore, how we connect that love with ourselves today is the issue at hand.

Then, will that love be in the highest place in the universe or in a low place? In other words, will it be in a high-pressure zone or a low-pressure zone? If this love is in the central place of a high-pressure zone, you must create a high-pressure zone within yourselves to reach that place. Without forming an equal high-pressure zone, you cannot approach it. Therefore, the only way to absorb this love and establish a relationship with it is to create a high-pressure zone.

How do we create that? Matthew 5:3 states that the poor are blessed. When the poor help those who are in the most need, they find themselves in a position to receive infinite love. Such people do not feel happiness from parental love, spousal love, or children's love, which are the kinds of love that humans often long for; instead, they feel an indescribable unhappiness. If those people possess a foundation of longing for essential and high-dimensional love, they cannot help but deny all realities and seek a new path. If there is only one way for new connections to be made, it must be done.

The Purpose of Faith
What path do all religions seek? They do not seek a path centered around national love. They seek a connection that transcends nations, aiming for a heavenly relationship. That path is not a smooth one; it is not a free path welcomed by all. It is a rugged path through valleys, a path of solitude. We must understand that it is also a path of solemn struggle alongside sorrow.

It is not because of a lack of money that one walks such a path. It is not because of a lack of food that one walks such a path. There is only one reason: it is the yearning for a cosmic love that can fully satisfy the heart. Seeking the one bridge that can connect to that love, one enters a realm where that love can be everything, walking that path to receive recognition from the Absolute. If there is such a realm where one can experience the love of the Absolute, it is not a dualistic realm but a singular realm. The direction—east, west, south, or north—is not the issue; the issue is what one seeks.

Until now, feeling empty and unfulfilled, one must have a subjective awareness that can fill that heart and overflow, connecting with the universe. Thus, one must reach a realm where they can feel peace, which possesses infinite value as an existence of infinite worth. To achieve this, one must encounter absolute love one-on-one.

When one views the universe from such a realm, that universe cannot leave one's embrace. Even if you and I are far apart, we can feel that we are in a direct relationship, and if such infinite love exists on this earth, how precious would that love be? That love cannot be governed by history. It cannot be governed by the present age. It cannot be governed by the future that is yet to come. We must have such a realm of love.

What is the purpose of those who walk the path of virtue today? They often say it is self-actualization. In other words, it is about completing one's life. Then, what will one do after completing life? One must encounter perfected love. After encountering perfected love, what will one do? One must enter a position where they can possess the factors of infinite happiness. To possess the factors of infinite happiness means to stand in a position that cannot be severed from infinite love. In other words, one must enter the realm of the love of the Absolute God.

A child who receives parental love cannot forget that love, even if they are far from their parents. No matter how complex the environment or how extreme the joy, they cannot forget that love. As long as the love of their parents, which cannot be exchanged for anything in the world, remains imprinted in their hearts, that child's heart cannot stray elsewhere. They are always in their parents' embrace; they cannot be anything other than their parents' child.

Similarly, if we live our lives taking the infinite love of God, which is the only one, as our foundation, we live with God. Even if a son or daughter who receives parental love is happy or sad, or finds themselves in difficult circumstances, if they think centered around that love and stimulate hope for tomorrow centered around that love, they will overcome everything, and the bond of love between parent and child will become unbreakable. The same goes for God. If we have established an absolute love relationship with God, we must feel gratitude for that love no matter what environment we find ourselves in, and we must reflect on everything centered around that relationship, feel centered around that relationship, and live centered around that relationship. Such a person cannot leave the realm of God's love. Only such a person can testify to God. When that person speaks of God's story, that story can resonate with God's inner workings. Seeking such a place is the path of virtue.

When is the time we can feel God's love most deeply?
What time can we be closest to that place on the path of virtue? Is it during the ignorant infancy, the mature adulthood, or the old age when one can weigh everything inside and outside the world? When we consider what that time is, it is like the period of adolescence.

During adolescence, one does not merely observe flowers; they extend their emotions and wish to relate the entire flower to themselves. When appreciating a particular tree, it does not end there; they wish to connect that appreciation to the entirety of nature. This heartfelt yearning emerges during adolescence. Among these, there is a time when one can draw a love object that can wholly captivate them, which is the essence of adolescence.

Where does the standard for personality perfection in the world of virtue come from? It comes from love. Personality perfection is achieved centered around God's infinite and absolute love. When should this love relationship be established? It should be established during a time similar to adolescence. When the adolescent-like emotions leave the realm of virtuous living, one becomes dry and uninteresting. At that point, the life of virtue will come to an end. A person who walks such a path must not have a boundary line appear before them. Only those who do not have such a boundary line can be assured and solidified in the infinite world. The motivation to achieve this is love.

When we see adolescent girls, they may cry upon seeing leaves fall. Why do they cry? It is because there is something within that captivates them in their own way. They feel that there is an infinite new connection involved. Though it may be symbolically and visually represented, they feel the infinite love connection within, which causes them to express such emotions unconsciously. This is a matter you should engrave in your hearts.

When you see the waves of the sea crashing on the shore, it feels as if the waves are hitting you, and when you look at nature, it seems as if all of nature is breathing, bringing joy to you. When you look at it joyfully, it appears as the highest symbol of joy, and when you look at it sadly, it can stimulate that sadness and, conversely, provoke new hopes from within that sadness.

If there is someone living in such a realm, pursuing infinite connections with such feelings, that person is not dry and uninteresting. When they find themselves in solitude, infinite connections appear like the essence of spring, even there. This realm of experience is the world of God's love.

You may spiritually experience such moments. What can I say? In the spring, when the haze rises over blooming flowers in a garden, surrounded by clouds and flowers, you may find yourself infinitely immersed in that atmosphere, savoring infinite value and entering such a realm.

At that time, you will undoubtedly feel a realm where you connect with the dynamic and static pulse of the universe, as if blood is being pumped from the heart. Even within a limited body, when you connect with the infinite realm from that limited state, you will feel the life that is connected to it. In that place, you will feel life itself. In that place, you will finally be able to feel an independent emotion regarding your own actions. Isn't that place of independent feeling the place of completion? God will rejoice when He sees humans in such a state.

Thus, Buddha described the place of completion as the absolute state of self-sufficiency. When one stands in a position of the highest conviction, acting independently, saying, "Everything I do is the most precious thing that can be absolutely guaranteed," they can possess a second subjective value. Advancing toward such a place is the most rewarding endeavor for us humans.

We must achieve a love that represents the whole.
That place cannot be transcended through knowledge or perception, nor can it be surpassed with external concepts. It cannot be transcended without the realm of love. You see, don't you? The eyes of someone who longs for another are different. The longing eyes are not flat but three-dimensional. When you see such eyes, you can immediately recognize it. A person who resonates with such relative factors has transcended their own perception. In this way, the foundation that allows us to transcend our own perception within the realm of sensation is emotional.

You must adopt a way of thinking centered around this emotion. When my hand moves, I should think not merely that energy is being expended, but that my hand moves to pursue something emotional. Also, why do I live? I should think it is to pursue a more valuable emotional goal.

In this light, engaging in a life of faith does not mean being alone and lonely. Moreover, having many people around does not mean they are all friends. There is only one person whose heart aligns with mine. Isn't that so? There is only one path that a person can take. When there is only one path, and it is said that we have united around the whole, one wants to boast about that whole. Isn't that right? When one finds an object of love that cannot be found in the world, when they truly find the one and only object of love in heaven and earth, they want to reveal it infinitely. How far do they want to reveal it? To the ends of heaven, to the infinite world, they want to reveal it forever. You must understand that the foundation of such a heart cannot exist without love.

If one loves only one person, that love is one-sided and biased. However, when two people love each other, they must be able to represent the whole. From this perspective, when a blessed family or an individual established in purpose says, "I love so-and-so" or "I love so-and-so's child," that love is one-sided. However, when two love each other, it becomes a love that represents the whole.
You will be in a position to replace the body. Only then can unification occur in that world. Without that, unification cannot happen. Even when you look at it centered around your family, whether it's Kim or Park, they are in a one-sided position until they find their own object of love. However, it should not end in a one-sided position. When it is said that they have become one from a one-sided position, they must represent the whole. To do that, a central love that encompasses the whole must be achieved. That is what you must do.

What is most needed for humans?
We are passing through the years of ten years as if they are fleeting. Think about how you have been since the first time you entered the church until now. How did you treat the teacher? You thought of the teacher as just another man. So, what could you gain through the teacher? No matter how much the teacher talks with your heart in mind, you evaluate the teacher externally as someone who teaches a certain truth in a specific field. When the teacher speaks from a position of having reached a limit where there is no other path to seek beyond being born as a human, there are people who complain about this and that. You should not view the teacher from a human perspective.

When we look at humans centered on God, we are merely a small dot. In terms of sand, we are just a single grain. We cannot represent the whole like that. However, we must be in a position to replace the infinite whole. To do that, there must be a backing of love. Without such love, no matter how much you have received teachings from the teacher, you will only be a successor. The teacher is merely a mentor who teaches you. If that is the case, once you learn everything the teacher has to teach, your connection with the teacher will end.

Therefore, there must be a connection of love in your heart that is as precious as the spring season. This must have the power to draw you in so that you cannot leave. There must be something unbreakable that relates you to the teacher or relates the teacher to God. If that is absent, a transformation will occur. An infinite division will take place. Originally, division is done for the sake of development. However, it goes in a state that is not like that. The problem lies here.

So, what has the teacher presented to you today? The content of the Unification Church principles? The teacher does not think so. He has presented the love of God that can overcome the pain of death even when entering the path of death.

What the teacher seriously thought about with Chairman Yoo Hyung-won was whether he had the content that could support such a thing. He suffered a lot for the teacher when he followed him. Among those times, he thought of the teacher a lot when the teacher was in prison. That is why when the teacher thinks of Chairman Yoo, he thinks, "He was such and such a person." He was drawn to the feeling of wanting to meet in the early morning while lying in the cell, and he had the internal support to value even a single note received. I remember him as such a chairman.

Then, what is most needed for us, who are scattered in the world of death, as we seek the original world we must go to while overcoming the path of death? It is not a matter of knowing a lot. 

Do you know the term "afterglow"? If you cannot be the very being that can shine with the afterglow like the emotional world, you must at least have a reflector of the afterglow. If you stand in a position where he is like this and I am like this as a reflector, that is fake. You must become one. You must enter a realm where you are completely one. For any mirror to reflect light completely, it must be free of blemishes. Only then can it reflect fully. That reflected afterglow must become an emotional afterglow. Thus, at all times, the direction of all my heart must completely align with the original light. When you stand in such a relative position, it is not two. The reflected light is the same as direct light.

Making humans eternal
As you go through your life, there must be a pursuit point in that life. It means there must be a net's edge. What is like the edge of a net in life? It is the love of God. When God's love drops anchor in me, I can go in and out of the infinite world. To feel such emotions, you must pray.

When you pray, even if you pray in Korea, you must pray for the family members scattered around the world. When you reach the realm of feeling God's heart, you will know what kind of feelings someone has without anyone explaining it to you. It must flow through subjective content to be eternal. The subjective content that determines this is love that can become the original connection of subjectivity, not relative content.

That is why you must pursue God's love even if you die. In your journey through life, what is the center of God's personality that you have been pursuing until now? It is not truth. The center is heart. You must enter a position that can transcend the peak of that heart. When you enter that position, the pain of your death will not be considered. It is the realm where all suffering can be overcome by God's love. How will you seek a position where you can connect with the power to overcome the dominion of death on this earth? This is the problem.

Therefore, whether you are eating, sleeping, working, or doing anything, you must think about this. Such a person is always someone who sings of spring days. He lives his life singing of spring days. Even if he is old, he does not recognize himself as old. Of course, everyone feels that way. There is a saying that living to a hundred is hard, but the heart does not feel that way. Your heart is the same, right? Even an old grandfather or grandmother has the heart of a young maiden or bachelor. Even if his wife is a wrinkled old woman, he does not want to call her an old woman. He thinks of the times when flowers bloomed as the standard. He wants to live with the heart that says, "You and I are one" until the day he dies, centered on the day they became a couple.

It is not that he looks ugly just because he is currently old; rather, he cherishes that feeling centered on the old connection and wants to embrace everything, wanting to wrap each other's lives with that love. Such a couple is a happy couple. Even if they have shrunk, there must be that heart that says, "My beloved person." If that heart is absent, that couple is a lonely couple. They are a couple that exists or does not exist. When you look at flowers, camellias cannot change. They have an unchangeable essence as camellias.

So, what does aging mean? When viewed from the perspective of humans, aging means moving toward a new world of spring. Although the body may be old, the fundamental love that blooms within is more beautiful than external things. Humans must have such love to be happy.

The relationship between parents and children is the same. When sons and daughters are young, they sit on their knees and raise them with great care, but as the children grow older, they cannot do that. However, parental love does not end just because the children are older. That love manifests even more dimensionally. The value of dedicating oneself centered on content that cannot be exchanged for one's life becomes more apparent as time goes on. If a son can discover the value of such parental love, he is a filial son even if he does not have the title of a filial son. Because of that, he pursues goodness, and because of that, when he can have hope for tomorrow beyond when he was young, that child becomes a filial son, doesn't he?

The path of heart, the path of love

To long for and seek such love does not happen just by going. When God is present in the place where the subject and object exchange, multiplication occurs. Without the spirit of absolute power intervening, multiplication does not happen.

When a woman and a man, that is, a couple, love each other, children are born. When should children be born? If that happens, undoubtedly, good and virtuous sons and daughters will be born. However, in today's fallen world, that has not happened. Has there been anyone who has given birth to children from a position where the heart that loves God centered on the nation and the world is internally aligned?
