In that sense, I have said while blessing you that by looking at your sons and daughters, you can see how faithful you have been before God and how much you live receiving God's love. Your sons and daughters testify to that. Therefore, you must become filial sons and daughters before God. You must also become devoted sons and daughters.

To become a devoted son, you must establish emotional connections that exceed that of a devoted son. To become a filial son, you must establish emotional connections that exceed that of a filial son. It must come from the depths of your heart. To do that, you must have such connections. You must inherit good heavenly qualities from your ancestors. To be someone who can practice devotion and filial piety is not a matter determined by your own generation, but it is determined based on the connections with dozens or hundreds of generations of ancestors. The same goes for viewing God's heart.

How joyful have you been to know this meaning? Have you ever been joyfully ecstatic? If you have not experienced joy, your heart's yearning for truth is stuck at a certain limit. You must go beyond that limit; you should not feel the limit.

In this universe, infinite power is in motion. This world moves because there is infinite power. When you look, it may seem like the wind is not blowing, but the wind is always blowing. We may not feel the wind blowing, but there is not a day without wind. There is no day that is completely still. Each field is functioning in a supplementary manner. When it is quiet, if you open the door, you can feel the air coming in through that door. It is moving without stopping.

You must understand that wherever there is air, there will be a positive and negative action. Those small actions gather together to form a cosmic great storm. Likewise, this cosmic realm also moves with a certain direction. The movement of the cosmic realm is centered around a small end. You must feel this.

You must go beyond the limit of the power that can perform physiological actions and establish a relationship with the infinite world. When that happens, your limits will disappear. Therefore, you must have a power stronger than the power derived from human physiological actions. When that happens, history unfolds. If humans cannot bear that, the power strikes humans, causing them to tilt.

In this world, there will be God's love. That is, there is an eternal element that can continue forever, just like our ideals. Without that, God could not have made humans into subjects centered on eternal love. If there is a way for God's love and today's humans to connect and relate, that way is not the way of truth, nor is it the way of hope. That way is the way of heart.

What kind of path is the path of virtue? It is the path that is filled with longing for the world of God and breaks away from the longing for the human world. As much as you love people, as much as you love your parents, as much as you love your spouse and children, you must love the world of God even more. That is the path of virtue. So how much should you love? You should reach a point where you can say that there is nothing better than this.

The feeling in the world of virtue is like this. A person who has received grace, a person who receives God's love, appears beautiful. When you receive love, you appear beautiful. How beautifully do you appear? You appear like light. Therefore, you can emit light. Similarly, when all beings emit such light, there are no unworthy people, that is, there are no ugly people.

Among the people of the world, when you see a couple, there may be some who seem mismatched. You might think, "How can such a handsome man live with such an ugly woman?" However, in that man's eyes, that woman appears as the most beautiful woman. This is because he has not found anyone beyond the person who gave him his first love, the one who poured 100% of their love into him, and he thinks that there is no one who can make him happier than her. However, if he had found someone who could give him more love than that, he would have gone to that person. Do you understand what I mean?

What is different about the Unification Church from other churches?
What makes our Unification Church different from the world is that it has presented a connection through which we can pour out a love that is more precious and valuable than anything in the world. It is not about the husband you love or the wife you love.

Have you thought about how much genuine love you have held until now and how much you have felt the teacher's love? Have you thought about that? It is not the rational love that people have today. Rational love is like a shadow. Do you have subjective love? That is the question. Even in longing, do you understand that there is a realm of longing? Even in a place where you desperately love, you must have a love that can long for again. That love is an infinitely giving love. Even if you clash and clash again, there is no end. Do you understand what I mean? It is not that it ends when you clash; it is a love that continues to dig deeper, saying you love it to death. Such love reaches the realm of completion.
Isn't there a place?  
The fundamental love of God in the universe, the universal love, that love of God  
has been reconciled with each individual human being from the time of the fall to today.

you rise in love, fall in love, or stumble in love, it can all be called love, right?

I, too, try to bury myself repeatedly. However, there are those who cannot do so. If you give for such people, both will break. Therefore, you must establish relative relationships well.

God longs for us with the original heart He had when He dealt with humanity before the fall. However, if I long for God with a fallen heart from a fallen position, can I meet God? Then how can I become someone who longs for God with the original heart? I must be absent. I must not think centered on myself. A person who thinks centered on themselves can never go to heaven. A dutiful child thinks of their parents first when something good happens, a loyal subject thinks of their king first, and a virtuous woman thinks of her husband first when something good happens. Why do we long for the early days? When considering all of this, the issue is the emotional standard. Emotion is a longing that does not cease. The teacher thinks that the time spent living with Wonpil in Beomnyeokgol was good. That was a good time. Which time during school was the best? Once you enter middle and high school, it is just indifferent, "Did you come?" and that is the end. Is that not so? You all say the 1960s were good. What was good about that time? Being scolded a lot, the teacher being dragged around, hiding every day in the north, south, east, and west, feeling your heart sink when someone comes looking for someone at the door, and feeling like your insides are melting—what was good about that time? Have you felt that? That being said, during that time, there was a living heart of mutual care. Because we felt that, we say that time was good. Why was that time good? The reason we must walk this path to the end

If you buy nice clothes and a house for one of your children among many and make him live well, but that child sells everything to share with his siblings, would you say, “Hey, you rascal!” and punish him? It is the same. I do not seek sympathy because I do what I enjoy. Do not pity me.

Among you, raise your hand if you have shed tears because you missed the leader. If there is someone who has not shed tears from missing the leader, that person is a fake. Yet, even now, not only the established churches but also those within the Unification Church headquarters do not understand what the leader is doing. 

There is a story that the leader cannot forget even now. You may not have such a story. When I was in Heungnam prison, I received a small amount of flour once a month. Since there were about 30 people in the cell, I could not share much, so I scooped a spoonful into pieces of newspaper and distributed it. The day we distributed the flour was a festive day. It was not about the beef ribs. A single bean there is better than ten oxen in the outside world. 

No matter how much someone tries to maintain dignity and status, when a bean falls, they instinctively reach out for it. About 20 people reach out at the same time, trying to grab the bean. You probably do not know that realm. You cannot even imagine it. Even when eating oil mixed with water, it is indescribably delicious. Why is that? Because the body lacks oil. Eating raw beans is also incredibly delicious. It is because the body lacks fat, so the absorption is strong. That is why it tastes so good. The degree of taste varies according to the strength of absorption. 

Therefore, when a bean falls, they rush to pick it up. That is physiological instinct. Most are starving, so they crawl to grab it. About 20 people fight over that single bean. The leader has seen many such situations. 

So how precious do you think the flour distributed in spoonfuls is? It is more valuable than all the wealth one possesses or a tiled house with nine doors. The day the leader distributes flour is indeed a festive day. 

The leader does not eat it alone out of greed. He absolutely does not eat it alone. He makes rice cakes from the flour and wraps them in newspaper to take to the workplace. He fasts until lunchtime, holding back his desire to eat, and the longing is immense. Still, he endures because he wants to share it. 

The night before, he has fasted, and even when he wakes up in the morning, he is still fasting, so while sweating and working, that is all he can think about. (Laughter) Then, as soon as the bell signaling lunchtime rings, people quickly rush to it. The factory is large, so it is divided into the first and second work areas, and there are several large fertilizer piles. During work hours, they work there, but...
For those 15 minutes of break time, that place is heaven. The life in that world is something that those who have not experienced it cannot understand. Such experiences cannot be exchanged for any amount of money because they are stained with blood and tears. That world is one where you must invest everything from your life.

After enduring such torture, the next day becomes a sad day and an unforgettable day. Even now, I sometimes think of that time. You do not know about that.

Furthermore, they do not know whether they are on the left or right side. They also do not understand the up and down relationships.

One must have a standard to gauge these before-and-after, left-and-right, and up-and-down relationships, and that standard is the heart. You must live with a firm standard such as, "God is my Father, and I am undoubtedly His son." This is a standard that cannot be denied by anything. Then, this will serve as a lubricant for moving all of my limbs and body. That is how the heart can be at ease. Otherwise, the heart is not at ease. Such a state is necessary. Without it, one cannot distinguish between good and evil properly. Those who have experienced this will find that their heart rejects anything that deviates even slightly from the principle.

To avoid losing grace, the teacher has never raised his voice against any practitioner until now and has listened to all their words. Then, one comes to understand to what degree that person has risen. One must recognize the unfortunate circumstances that God has not been able to address until now and stand in a position that understands their circumstances better than anyone among the many practitioners they have sought out. Then, they will open up all their good and bad aspects. Once those things are settled, they will follow me. Thus, when the day comes to launch a joint offensive in a new field, greater development can occur.

However, if that person does not think there is a way to rise higher through the teacher and insists that what they have brought out until now is the best, the closest, and the most comfortable, and tries to pull me there, I cannot be dragged along. If that happens, a separation will occur. It has been that way until now. Just the other day, I met such a person. The way to judge the many practitioners in the world of morality is like this. For example, if there is a son, it depends on whether that son is like Esau or like Jacob. Esau believed that going hunting, catching sheep, and offering gifts was a way to show filial piety to his parents. However, Jacob monopolized his mother's love while staying at home. This shows how important the emotional aspect is.

From this standpoint, the teacher tries to establish a relative connection through the process that practitioners have walked and give them something beyond that, but they do not receive it, so I end up taking it away. Then, they lose all the process they have walked. It is like someone who has studied for ten years becoming a mere wooden Amitabha Buddha. The teacher is conducting such a strategy.

You are in the same position. When a practitioner shares their circumstances with you, listen to all of it, and then say, "What about this and that? Aren't you in this position?" Based on that emotional standard, the practitioner will resonate. However, the problem is whether that practitioner is a leader who can guide higher based on God's heart. In moving forward with God's heart, one cannot center on oneself. Centering on oneself is not the way of filial piety or loyalty. One must absolutely prioritize God. If that center is misaligned, then from there, they will be stopped. That is how it is.

Therefore, one must discern whether it started from heaven or from earth, whether it is centered on God or on oneself. No matter how good the explanation is, if it is explained centered on oneself, it must be cut off. Even if one feels that the explanation based on their experiences is more valuable, the question is whether the path they are taking is centered on themselves or on God's providence. If it is centered on oneself, one must not be taken away but rather take away from that person. That is why the struggle in the spiritual world is so difficult.

As you all know, how many people have come directly to the teacher until now? The teacher has acknowledged all the efforts those people have made for heaven and treated them as honored guests. In the historical process, one must stand as someone who values God more than anyone else, and that is why I have treated them with all my heart. If I have done that, shouldn’t they know who this teacher is? Until the point where their capacity is filled, I have given to them, but from that point on, shouldn’t they be for the teacher? If they cannot stand in a position of service, they will lose everything. In this way, the teacher has taken away all the grace that God has laid out until now.

The string that can bind heaven’s principles and human principles is what the teacher is exploring regarding the many spiritual people of various denominations. Thus, one comes to know their history. The teacher knows the histories of Pastor Gil Seon-joo and Pastor Lee Yong-do as well. He knows what kind of mission they came as in what era. When their mission period ends, this must be handed over.

However, the transfer cannot be done from man to man. It must be done through a woman. Furthermore, a woman cannot transfer to another woman. It must be done through a man. This is how it is exchanged and developed. It is to have a better emotional connection. Therefore, if it is a woman, she must govern the man alone, and if it is a man, he must govern the woman alone. In doing so, one must find a common emotional point to be determined as a perfect filial son or perfect filial daughter. However, people do not understand this.

That is why the teacher shared with the members of the religious council the essence of what the Unification Church has struggled with and developed until now. There are heavenly principles and human principles, but what will these heavenly and human principles be centered on? Heavenly principles seek human principles, and human principles seek heavenly principles, but what is the string that can bind these together? It is neither truth nor any power. The only thing that can bind this is when a person seeks God, and God seeks the person, allowing them to become one. What kind of place is that? It is a place where a person can call God their Father and where God can call a person their son or daughter. There is no higher position than this.

From that perspective, Jesus Christ proclaimed the heavenly principles, which are the highest emotional core for humanity. He spoke of the bride and groom as a horizontal standard and then mentioned brotherhood.

Since God is an emotional God, the only way to be invited by God is through the standard of being a son or daughter, where the three types of love—parental love, spousal love, and children's love—are realized. In this regard, the Unification Church has presented the three types of love centered on the family, which is a great thing and serves as a model in the world of morality.

The reason Christianity, centered on Jesus Christ, will remain until the end times is because of this. What can endure until the end is love. That is why the Bible states, "And now these three remain: faith, hope, and love. But the greatest of these is love." (1 Corinthians 13:13) So, what is the string of love that can connect to the closest position with God? In other words, what is the link that can bind heavenly principles and human principles? It is the relationship between father and son.

A religion that can call God Father and has the emotional content that God can call humans sons and daughters is a world religion. That religion is Christianity.

Where can humans find happiness with God? Humans seek emotional happiness through religion. So, when will the door to happiness be wide open for humans? In other words, what is the place where humans can dance the happiest, sing the happiest, and rejoice the most? It is not a place of great wealth or global authority. It is the place where one finds back a beloved son or daughter after losing them for a thousand years, where a beloved couple breaks down the walls that prevented them from meeting due to enmity and can meet each other, and where a family that was captured by enemies is completely liberated and can meet again. There is no greater joy than that.

Therefore, what kind of world will the restored world of emotions be? It will be the world where a son rejoices in meeting the father who has been lost for six thousand years, and where the father can embrace and love that son. There cannot be a happier world than this. This becomes the ideal foundation for all humanity and the basis like leaven. That is why the emotional aspect is so important.

In what position does God want to love humans? He does not want a position like that of a king and his subjects. God wants to love from the closest position, the position of father and son or daughter. Our Unification Church’s principles teach this. Therefore, no matter who offers the world, if they speak words that deviate from this principle, do not listen to them. There is nothing else. Words can be fabricated in countless ways. Any person with even a little inspiration can fabricate stories. Such people can manipulate others into responding as they think.

Thus, the problem is how much their emotional standard aligns with God in a relative relationship, and how much it is in agreement vertically. That is the issue. Therefore, you must pass through that standard. Then, there is freedom there. That is why one must become the sons and daughters of God. This is the principle.

For this purpose, our Unification Church aims for individual restoration, then for the completion of marriage, and finally for the completion of the family through the multiplication of good children.

Humans must receive God's love as sons and daughters centered on the vertical standard. Only then can a complete vertical standard be established through that connection, and a complete horizontal standard can be established centered on that. It is possible to derive 360 degrees centered on 90 degrees. That is why the relationships of up and down, front and back, and left and right centered on emotional relationships are the issues.

The Way of Love

Therefore, you must live for your partner in married life. As mentioned before, love is not yours. Loving your children is not yours either. It is God's. God's love flows out through me. It is to leave God's love for a thousand years and beyond. That is why you must not steal that love. Do not digest it as your own love to satisfy your own desires. It must be returned to God.

Until now, practitioners have thought that once they reach a certain standard, they could boast of themselves and believe they could do anything. They think that God's power is upon them, allowing them to do anything. However, that is a million miles away from the truth. The path of love is not about performing powers. The path of love begins with doing the most difficult tasks. Do you understand?

People who pray in the mountains are all saying that the time has come. Yes, the time has come. So now they say they will seek the master. The person I met the other day was such a person. At that time, that person said it was their time, which is why they met me, and they wanted me to recognize how sincere they had been. What do I have to recognize? If I want to recognize, I will, and if I don't want to, I won't. That is entirely up to me. Love cannot be obtained through coercion or threats. It must be connected in a sincere and free environment. The heart of fear must not intervene. In the path of such love, it is acceptable to die. To break through the realm of death's love and enter a new realm of love, one must receive the shock of love that can deny their fallen self, born of the blood of death. That is the problem.

That is why those gathered here must pray a lot to establish this direction. Through prayer, reflect on which group you belong to. Consider whether you are an intellectual person, a volitional person, or an emotional person. There are these three types of people. One must recognize whether they are an intellectual person...
Do not claim to be intellectual; you must seek out static individuals. Therefore, we are establishing the Trinity in our Unification Church. 

The Trinity is not composed of people with the same character. Each individual possesses their own unique personality. It is about bringing together different people into one. The organization of the Trinity is meant to go through a training process to create unity. 

What our members must understand is that the era focused on family life is now over. For example, the time when Kim Won-pil lived centered around his personal living environment has passed; now we must develop the responsibility of creating the living environment of the Trinity. 

In that sense, I feel that Chairman Yoo has done well in the spiritual world. Now, Chairman Kim Young-hwi must understand that the family of Gilja (史吉子) should not be pitiful. In the spiritual world, those families must unite. If the three generations centered on the Teacher do not become one, they cannot enter the spiritual world. The Trinity must go through three generations to be established, and through the principles of that Trinity, we will reach the ideal world. Isn’t that right? Therefore, Chairman Yoo Hyung-won should not think of his children separately from his own children. 

So, the issue is love. In 1 Corinthians 13, it says, “Prophecies will cease, tongues will be stilled, knowledge will pass away; but love remains.” Even if you have the ability to move mountains, that will all pass away, so do not believe in it. The question is, how much heartfelt love do you possess? When looking at your nation, have you become someone who can forget your own reason and shed tears out of pity for your people? This is a difficult issue. The problem is not how to persuade others with truth to create your own people; the issue is how you have become. You must always think about these things. 

When you pray in the name of the True Parents, what is that true love, and who are the True Parents? Do not think of that only in relation to the Teacher and Mother. Think of the True Parents as a level that transcends national sentiments and embraces the world, where they can sincerely love all people as one. That is why the Teacher also prays in the name of the True Parents. 

Living in the world of heart 
When dealing with all people, you should not approach them with greed. In the world of virtue, the one who appears weakest often wins over the strong. This is also true in the world. Those in high positions are often undermined by those around them. Therefore, one must always stand in a low-pressure state. The Teacher speaks powerfully when addressing you in public, but when alone, he takes on the position of a child. He stands in the position of a child before the Father. Even in prayer, one should have the heart that longs for the embrace of their parents. As a mature leader of the Unification Church, it is not about wanting to take responsibility in this way. That position is unstable and cautious. Because I take responsibility in place of God, if I make a mistake, I will immediately face Satan’s accusations. However, when I am like a child, God protects me. I can stand in a position to receive God’s compassion. The flow of air moves from high pressure to low pressure. Therefore, you must stand in the low-pressure realm of heart. Thus, you need the heart that longs for the embrace of your parents, like a child. 

To do this, you must pray. From now on, I will have you pray. Anyone who prays can have spiritual experiences. Among you, there are those whom God loves, that is, those who are at the forefront emotionally. To you, they may seem insignificant, but they can be emotionally first. In this way, the world of virtue is always about heart. 

The world lives through the bonds of heart. It is not through the bonds of truth that the world lives, but through the bonds of heart. There is a hymn we sing that reflects this, right? The world lives through the bonds of heart, and it is through the bonds of nature that we are united as one. It is through the bonds of heart that we can finally be unified. That is the bond of nature that unites us. From there, an eternal bond that can be exchanged is formed, allowing for eternal exchange. Isn’t that right? What comes after the line about eternal exchange? “Our homeland.” It is our homeland, the world of nature. What comes next? “On the foundation of happiness, we will live forever. We are the pride of the warriors of unification, gathering our hearts to strive forward.” This is what it means to be a warrior of unification. The lyrics may seem difficult, but the content is all principled. Think carefully and sing it. 

The world lives through the bonds of heart. It is impossible to live only by truth without the bonds of heart. So, do you prefer intellectual people or static people? “I prefer static people.” Knowledge disperses and causes one to forget oneself. On the other hand, heart creates unity. Knowledge is like spreading out a cloth, while heart is like wrapping it up. When you spread it out, you cannot carry it all at once, but when you wrap it up, you can carry it all at once. When it is spread out, it appears numerous, but when it is combined, it becomes one. Where there is oneness, there can be no conflict. 

Therefore, when you see those who claim to know something, they are neither Socrates’ disciples nor anyone else’s; they belong nowhere. They become disconnected from their own nature. Such people are full of twists and turns. A person who becomes isolated like this is a significant problem even in the spiritual world. They cannot find their place and are always wandering around. Therefore, you should strive to be static rather than intellectual. Be the kind of person who, when someone reaches out to hold your hand, can feel their body and heart tremble and shed tears. This is also true in the world of virtue. God is like this too. 

Faithful people must be indifferent to material things. 

We have now entered the late 1970s. It is August in the solar calendar and July in the lunar calendar; at this point, we must engage in self-reflection. Right now, I do not see any desire for purpose among you. I see no confidence burning with the belief that you can break through mountains for the hope of tomorrow. Therefore, we must engage in self-reflection. 

Why have we become like this? Is it because the path we have walked until now has been wrong, or is it because the Teacher’s guidance methods are flawed? If the Teacher’s guidance methods are not wrong, then why have we ended up like this? There is a problem here. What is that problem? It is whether I have lived publicly or privately. We must analyze and critique ourselves based on that issue. 

Was I pursuing the public good, or was I pursuing private interests? Did I start out pursuing the public good and then turn back to private interests? If you go out publicly and then revert to private interests, you will inevitably be broken. No matter how much effort you put in here, it will be of no use. When people engaged in faith deal with material issues, it is easy for them to come to an end. If someone who has been dealing in the spiritual realm pours all their concepts into the material realm, they are likely to come to an end. This is because the more public aspect is the spiritual. 

From this perspective, while our total sales business has helped externally, it has caused significant internal damage. That is why the Teacher stopped paying salaries from December of last year until now. Yet, there are still troubles among the business members and troubles among the district leaders. Those district leaders should be left behind. No matter how much they try to develop that area, they will not be able to. That is how I see it. If such people are here, they must repent. 

You must prioritize God over money. Even if I am running a business, if it collapses all at once, I will not shed a single tear. I have worked diligently on this business for ten years, but I will not shed a tear just because it collapses at once. If the business were to suddenly catch fire and disappear, what would I do? Even if I were to enter a higher realm than that, I would not care. 

Right now, there are machines in the factory that cost over five million won and some that cost seven million won. The Teacher does not want to boast about having newly acquired those machines. The issue is that those machines are merely a means. They are not the main course we must pursue. Just as you cannot go straight up Namhansanseong but must go up and down, material things are just one method. (Explaining while writing) In walking this path, material things are a plus for me. However, if I only focus on this, I will simply come down. Do you understand what I mean? You must understand that material things exist for God. 

A denomination that fights over the offerings placed on the altar will perish. In such a place, God does not dwell. Do you understand what I mean? In other words, if you build a church and then fight over it, God has already left that place. To move from a spiritual center to a material center, you must overcome many things. You must leap. However, to leap, you must overcome various difficulties. 

That is why the Teacher has emphasized overcoming spiritually since the 1960s. God has supported you in overcoming that. Not a single person has starved to death. Where has anyone starved to death? 

Think of God’s principles first. 

You must prioritize the church over yourselves. You should think that the need for money is to build the church more splendidly. Do not think that it is for your own household to prosper. Shouldn’t the foundation of the church be better than your own home? You need money to contribute something more valuable to the church, not to add to your own living expenses to live well. 

And you must think of God’s principles. You are connected to the Teacher in a relationship of benefactor and beneficiary, and you have managed money through the Teacher until now. Then, wouldn’t it be filial duty to help the Teacher? If you have difficulties here, how much more difficult must it be for the Teacher, who is in a public position? If you have used public funds, that is something that cannot be forgiven. God has already left that person. Of course, there may be circumstances… 

Even a murderer or robber has their reasons. Let’s say there is a robber who, unable to eat seaweed soup after his wife gives birth, is forced to hold a knife to someone’s chest to steal money. He might think that he is not bad when centered on his personal circumstances, but from a public perspective, that is bad. The motivation behind the crime, whether it is private or public, determines the size of the sin. This is the principle of sin. 

From that perspective, when I think of you all until now, you may have no face before the Teacher. The Teacher has been doing this for over ten years in Seoul alone, but when have you ever bought him a house? It is principled to buy at least one thing that the Teacher would cherish before preparing for your own living. Even if you get a room, you should first secure a room for God and then get a smaller room. Have you thought about that? All of these things are problems. 

The Teacher is now thinking of building houses for blessed families and churches. However, this is not the Teacher’s job; it is your job. If the Israelite people had fulfilled their responsibilities, the altar would have simply remained. Isn’t that so? If the Israelite people had fulfilled their responsibilities, the churches would have been built. From this perspective, building the church is not my responsibility. However, because you cannot take responsibility, and because your children have become disabled, the parents must inevitably suffer losses to provide for them. That is not a good position at all. Yet, you are all fighting over even a little more money. 

Foreign members would want their donations to be used for the Teacher. They would hope that after the Teacher uses it, it would be used through you. They give donations with that hope. Do you understand what I mean? That is the heavenly law. It is the way of heaven. Even if the Teacher does not use it and spends it all on his children, that is up to the Teacher, but that is not the principle. That is setting up some hypothetical condition. Therefore, you must always live with that public standard in mind. 

In district leader meetings or department head meetings, have you ever thought, “This month, let’s gather at least a penny to prepare a gift for the Teacher. If there are eight districts, let’s do a fundraising campaign in those eight districts, and even though we have not properly done anything for the Teacher until now, let’s do at least one thing.” Have you ever thought of such a thing? Without such thoughts, you are only thinking of how to get a little more profit from the company for your own convenience. This is worldly thinking. 

Was I public or private? 

The quantity does not matter. Each of you must gather your hearts to respond to God. If you have received, you must return. You are like toads that eat flies, only taking in. If you have received, you must give back. It is not the quantity that matters, but the sincerity of the whole. But have you returned? You have all these issues. 

You all know that the Teacher goes in and out of the factory day and night. For years, he has gone to the factory without missing a single day. I did not do this to earn a few bucks. It was for the Republic of Korea to prosper in the future and to bestow material blessings on this nation. The Teacher’s prayers have influenced the first and second five-year economic development plans of the Republic of Korea. Do you understand what I mean? This has happened because heavenly fortune has come. You must understand that. 

Therefore, our Unification Church members must endure hardships. It is natural to endure hardships. It is because we have deviated from the law that we must endure hardships. If you continue like this, many of your children may end up disabled. There may be many cases of polio or paraplegia among your children, and I am worried about that.
is what arises. Therefore, you must criticize yourself. You should evaluate whether you were more public or private, focusing on the distinction between public and private matters. The teacher handles everything in this manner. This is how the heavenly way is discerned. Suppose there is a person who is my enemy. Even so, when I deal with him, I do not approach him with the past enmity in mind. Even an enemy can contribute to the public world. The issue is which of our public standards, his or mine, is greater. If mine is greater, then even if I block him, I will not be violating the law. However, if I center my actions around my own desires and say, "You did this to me in the past, so now you should suffer," then that is no different from the world. We must judge all things with that perspective in mind.

In the future, the Japanese economy will revive. It is destined to revive. So where will the money of that time be spent? It will all come into the Unification Church and be used through the teacher. As the teacher has outlined all policies regarding Asia, Japan will undoubtedly develop and become entangled with us. Why is that? Because Japan has drained the blood and flesh of the Korean people. For nearly 40 years, it has been so, and thus it can be extended to hold responsibility for up to 400 years. Even if it does not extend to 400 years, can we not draw upon God's love for 40 years?

In the future, the number of Unification Church members in Japan will surpass that in Korea. This is based on population ratios. If the number of members in Japan is double that of Korea, they can easily support the Korean Unification Church members. Do you understand? "Yes." If such a situation arises, will Korea and Japan become one or not? Think about it. For example, if two Unification Church families in Japan can support one Unification Church family in Korea, will Korea and Japan remain enemies? The past enmity will naturally be forgotten. We are entering into such a time. That is why I do not worry even if we currently have nothing.

Thus, the teacher has said that the Japanese church should not use economic resources centered on Japan. Now that we are entering a national relative era, it is essential to receive approval from the teacher. That is why there has been personnel movement this year. Since last year, I have been receiving all economic reports and holding authority over personnel decisions. This is for the sake of the whole rather than just for Japan. It is more for Asia. Because it is more public to act for Asia than for Korea or Japan, we must make economic investments for Asia. When that happens, Asia will naturally become entangled due to the economic conditions invested. If we put in that effort, it will come to pass. In this way, when you criticize yourselves, always consider the issue of public and private matters.

Has your public standard developed or regressed? How should you change from the 1960s and 70s, before and after receiving blessings, centered around your intentions? This is the issue. When comparing before and after receiving blessings, how should it be? That is the question.

From that standpoint, the teacher has abandoned family and children for the sake of the will. There was no objection to that. You all know this. Yet, can you not abandon your children or your spouse? It is not about simply abandoning them. If it is for the sake of the will, even if families live apart, they will never starve. They are destined not to starve. However, if you insist on holding onto them, the situation will only worsen.

The teacher has lived this way. It is about entrusting everything to God. "Do as You will," and completely entrust yourself before God. And you must devote all your efforts to the public good. Do not center on material things. Even when evangelizing, do not consider whether the person to be evangelized has money or not. Seek out people of heart. A person who seems like a beggar to you could be the firstborn son of a wealthy family. It is wrong to prefer someone who is economically better than others. That is trivial.

You must understand that there is a difference between the public standards that God sees and the standards you hold. If you cannot develop from this point, you will ultimately become isolated and end up in a lonely place where you cannot even move, and no one will sympathize with you. In that case, you will regret having joined the Unification Church and regret having given up your beautiful youth until now. I foresee that happening. Therefore, I urge you to once again criticize and reflect on yourselves centered around the issue of public and private matters.

When looking back at the zeal you had for public standards before receiving blessings in the 1960s compared to the zeal you have now after receiving blessings and having families, have you developed or regressed? What about you? If you have regressed, you would have caused erosion in all your environments regarding public positions. If you look at economic conditions instead of God, you will be doomed. That household will ultimately be unable to stand anywhere. Such households will eventually come to realize this.

In the world of morality, it is said that one must abandon material things. You cannot serve both material and God. That is the principle. Personally, you may be able to do so, but can you do it as a family? If you cannot do it as a family, you cannot restore your family.

When looking at organizations, you must be in a position to say, "The money our Unification Church has can be used for the country." If you cannot stand in that position and say, "This is ours, and it cannot be denied," then the Unification Church cannot develop any further. If you do so, you will not have the heavenly foundation to overcome economic issues as the Unification Church. Isn’t that so?

Furthermore, when looking at the Republic of Korea, if the economic foundation of the Republic of Korea is absolutely necessary for the world, and when asked to "Use all of the Republic of Korea's budget for the world. Do charity work," if you say, "We cannot do that," then the Republic of Korea will perish. This is the path to go for heaven.

That is why the teacher has often told you that the Unification Thought must play a leading role in selling the Republic of Korea to buy the world. Therefore, the question is whether Unification Thought can provide ideological support for 30 million people. If it can, then after selling this country to buy the world, we will buy this country back again. When the day comes to circle the world, this country will be worth ten thousand times more. Then, there will be no business greater than that.

The teacher has come this far. When I first embarked on this path, I had never worn new clothes. I bought only second-hand clothes. I know well what my body is like. I am someone who is qualified to wear the most luxurious clothes and can also show off. However, when I look at the reality of many people suffering and unable to eat, my conscience does not allow it. When I occasionally wore new clothes, I felt so guilty that I could not even go outside. It is in my nature. When I see someone flaunting in new clothes, I find it strange. I wonder what kind of person they are. It is fundamentally different from such people.

The teacher has devoted all material possessions belonging to me to pursue a single public spiritual world. In doing so, I have laid a victorious foundation in the spiritual realm individually, but the question remains: how will I handle the family? When asked if I can make my beloved son and wife suffer for the sake of the nation, I must say, "I can." Then, at the most difficult time, God's command will come down. This is the time of indemnity. God commands us to do what ordinary people cannot do, especially when we are in the most difficult situations.

In fact, when I started this path, I did not have any particular plan. There is Seongjin here, but it was when Seongjin's mother was about 21 or 22 years old. I had no relatives, no rice, and not a penny to my name. So, I set out at dawn with a backpack to buy rice in Baekcheon, Hwanghae Province, when I received God's command. Would I go the way for my family, or would I go the way for the public God? I decisively chose, "I will go the way for heaven," and followed God's command to the North. That was a crucial turning point. Even after going to the North, I did not send a single letter home. It was not because I did not think of it; it was because it would not be good to do so. It is about completely clearing things up. We must go through that process. In this way, we Unification Church members must also be able to go forth while abandoning our families and giving up all our possessions.

Unification Church members must always be prepared to endure hardship. Recently, there have been rumors that the Unification Church has a lot of money. However, we must be able to sell all this property and return to nothing. We must be able to return to nothing for the sake of many religious organizations. When asked, "Can you return to nothing?" you must say, "I can." By doing so, you can lay the foundation for victory in the spiritual world. This is the principle.

Do you understand what I mean? That is why the teacher sees your suffering favorably. You must endure hardship. When the time comes to find the nation, you must come forth. If there is a way for the Republic of Korea to survive, then with all your possessions, whether it is for the Republic of Korea, Africa, or the world, you must do charity work and pray for them with your bare body, hoping that the will of Jehovah, the King of Hosts, may be conveyed to them. This is akin to Jacob going to meet Esau. If Jacob had offered useless servants and trivial possessions, Esau's heart would never have turned. The spiritual world does not turn.

What the teacher is currently worried about is the future economic issues. In the next one or two years, our Unification Church may face difficulties in Korea, but abroad, economic support will come to Korea. If necessary, I can borrow the strength of foreign countries to help this nation. Why? Because they are all citizens of the heavenly kingdom. For the establishment of that country, the teacher intends to mobilize all material resources from each nation.

The material blessings of the national era can only be received by those who have offered material sacrifices in the tribal era. Those who have not done so cannot receive those blessings. Do you understand? Even when the material blessings come in the global era, those who did not sacrifice materially in the national era cannot receive those blessings. What we need to prepare for 

Let’s say we weigh 3 billion people against a small number of us. The weight of the object...
When weighing, the heavier the object, the further away the weight on the scale must be placed to achieve balance. Placing the weight further away to achieve balance indicates that there is a lot of burden on the scale. 

Then, the question arises: Are we in a position to achieve balance with our nation or the world? The issue is whether you can play the role of the weight on the scale. No matter what weight you are measuring, you must act as the weight on the scale that can achieve balance with it. Since the weight is heavy, we must adjust the weight on the scale further away, and since it is light, we must have the capacity to adjust the weight on the scale closer. When considering this issue, we ourselves have not yet reached that state.

If you are currently around 35 years old, in just 15 years, you will be 50. That period of 15 years is brief. If you add another 15 years to that 50, you will be 65. You will be looking towards 70. No matter how hard a person looking towards 70 works, a third party does not recognize it. That person already feels like the sun is setting toward the western mountains. No matter how vigorously the sun shines and radiates heat, if you think of it as a slanting sunset, you lose interest in it. Just as people are very interested in the sun rising in the morning but have no interest in the light of the setting sun, we will find ourselves in a similar position.

Therefore, we must not allow the time of the sunset to come before us, standing in the forefront like an elite unit and establishing a tradition. So, how can we prevent that time from coming? We must create an environment where we can influence the nation before that time arrives.

But how do we create that environment? This is a significant issue. It does not mean that we should take up arms and do something. We must always be engaged in sowing seeds. Even if others reap, we must not be slow in sowing seeds.

From this perspective, how many years will you truly work? In the future, we must work in a compressed manner. Then the question becomes how to work in a compressed manner. Looking at the history of the Unification Church, there was a time of persecution at first, followed by a buffering period. We are currently in that buffering period. When a person takes the initiative against another, they will inevitably adopt a responsive posture without realizing it. It is physiologically that way. Therefore, we must take a defensive posture; if we do not, we will lose. We will simply be occupied.

God's Operation to Achieve Restoration

You must think about God's operation up until now. God's operation refers to the overall operation. God always conducts the overall operation based on individual operations. He seeks to connect point operations that stimulate individuals to line operations. However, there must be struggle in the process from point operations to line operations. Most people do not win in this struggle and become exhausted in the process.

Laying the foundation in point operations does not happen in a short time. Sometimes it may take a lifetime and still not succeed. It may take several generations. Then, how do we connect that point that has been prepared over several generations?

For this reason, God has chosen a specific nation to carry out His providence. He has been working through a specific nation. It is nearly impossible to conduct a global point operation and connect it to a line operation, which is why He has chosen a specific nation to conduct point operations. He injects powerful and spiritual energy into that nation to present new problems to humanity. 

What is presented at that time is not for the benefit of any particular organization but for the benefit of the whole. The question is how to show this.

No matter how much we claim to act for the whole and try to demonstrate it, this fallen world is entirely contrary to the world of God's providential purpose. Therefore, what was said to be for the whole ultimately becomes for the satanic world.

Looking at the satanic world, the work they do can never be seen as for the whole. They always attempt to achieve their goals centered around individuals while claiming to be for the whole. For this reason, those who stand in opposition to their goals have faced personal persecution, organizational persecution, and national persecution until now.

The reason the fate of religious organizations has been more miserable than that of any general organization in the historical era is that they had no supporters. Everyone thought they were distant from them and remained bystanders.

Let us examine the Roman era from this perspective. Near Rome, there is a catacomb that stretches for 20 kilometers. During the time of the early church, 70 disciples and the 12 apostles used that place to spread the gospel in Rome because at that time, Rome was the center of culture and could move the world based on law.

However, they also had their weaknesses. At that time, Rome was at a crossroads, trying to move towards humanistic thoughts centered around the foreign Greek civilization and liberal tendencies, leading to various divisions.

However, the Jewish nation was not like that. Centered around Judaism, they achieved unity, so early church believers had no place to stand. Thus, they had no choice but to seek places where they could stand among the Gentiles. However, even in that environment, the entire nation was persecuting them, so they dug into caves to escape.

If Rome had been like today's communist countries, they would not have survived. They could have blocked the back door of the cave and set fire to the front door or sprayed water through a hose to catch them all. However, the fact that they lived without being caught shows that even during the 400 years of harsh rule in Rome, there was some support and research for Christianity behind them.

The inside of the cave is entirely a cemetery. The cave is all a graveyard. When you look inside the cave, everything is tied up and made like shelves. They would wrap the corpses and leave them there. They could not bury them because they were dead, so they lived among the decaying bodies that smelled. They overcame such a miserable environment. The external people absolutely did not sympathize with them. The more they were not sympathized with, the more they sympathized with each other and bonded strongly.

When they encountered all the problems of the world—issues that humans can think about and ponder—or reflected on their experiences, they did not lose sight of their purpose. They thought that the reason they were placed in such a miserable environment was solely for one goal. That one goal was that humans must achieve eternal life, that is, they must seek the eternal world. They lived underground, focusing on how to overcome this catastrophe centered around that goal. Living underground is indeed a miserable thing.

Who would have thought that Christianity, which started from such a foundation, would move the world today? From this, we can see that God has carried out a powerful history centered around a specific race or specific individuals. You must understand this.

God is in a position where He cannot connect point organizations to the overall line organization. Because He could not carry out such activities, He created a specific position from which to establish a specific chosen people. Thus, among Christians, they formed relationships that no one else in the world could form, and even in situations where life and death were at stake, they had a united strength to care for one another. This could not be severed even by the most powerful forces of Rome. Even with the power of the sword and authority, it could not be cut off. Whenever they were cut off, they would reunite. They struggled for hundreds of years to cut them off, but they always came back together. They always had that resilience. That is not human power. It is solely God's power.

Because they had this strength, even though the period of Roman persecution during the early Christian church was long, they could overcome it. They suffered and faced persecution for 400 years, but the stronger the persecution, the more they united and resolved to overcome that trial. God's Will and America's Path

In light of this history, if God did not exist, it would be one thing, but since God exists, why does He govern in this way? It is because extending the path that humanity is currently on to lead them to the world of hope they envision is not God's will. God's providence and will are to turn humanity around all at once at the end of the world. Therefore, the current circumstances are not meant to drive humanity into a world of tragedy but to create a time when humanity can turn away from all external conditions they desire and return to an internal world centered on God.

Looking at the United States, which is considered a developed country, as you know, there are many wayward youths like hippies. They have no relatives, let alone parents. Moreover, they have no sense of national identity, worldview, or love for humanity. No matter how much you talk to them, it remains abstract and conceptual, and they cannot find anything that resolves the desires of their inner selves. As they try to keep pace with the external cultural world, they ultimately lose themselves and the whole.

They believe that the results they have brought about are due to external society and circumstances, not their own faults. Therefore, they do not joyfully accept the well-equipped external environment culturally but rather rebel against it. The factor that strongly reinforces their self-denial is the external cultural forms, which is why phenomena like the hippie movement arise. We know this all too well.

Under the current system of democracy, which emphasizes extreme individualism, there is no further path to take. The only way forward is to turn back. Therefore, the only way to find a new world is to return to the path of rediscovering the God that has been lost.

Humanity's Desire for Liberation

Considering this, the Republic of Korea, which has suffered for nearly 40 years under Japanese oppression, can be said to have experienced liberation from historical bondage. However, that liberation pertains only to the Republic of Korea and has nothing to do with the liberation of the world.

Moreover, we celebrated the 25th anniversary of liberation on August 15th yesterday. However, that was merely a liberation for the Republic of Korea from Japanese oppression, a necessary liberation to establish a new foundation for our nation to determine its own fate, but it does not significantly contribute to the ongoing historical process or the realm of bondage.

So, what do we and humanity desire? We hope for a day of global liberation that is revered by all humanity, rather than merely the liberation of our nation that we celebrated yesterday. Therefore, it becomes a question of when such a day will come. This question cannot be resolved based on material conditions but must be centered on inner, spiritual conditions, and how to guide a stronger force, a third authority, into existence.

What will accomplish this? Some ideology or religion must fulfill this task, but when we consider whether religion or ideology possesses the strength to do so, we conclude that it is impossible based on the forms that have already been tested and passed. Thus, the greatest news that all humanity yearns for, the blessed news, is nothing other than the "liberation" of the second and third liberation.

God as the Subject of Human Liberation

In the western United States, there are many hippies. In 1965, while passing through a street in San Francisco, I saw a young person standing still, looking up at the sky. After about four hours, I returned to that same street, and that person was still standing there in the same posture. I wondered what that person might be thinking. Perhaps he had many thoughts about himself or the countless people passing by. A more meaningful person might have thought about the future of America, and a broader thinker might have contemplated the world. A more serious individual might have pondered questions about the existence of God.

Standing there, that person might have been unable to find satisfaction in his own state.
As one feels more and more that they are not living up to their potential, they will ponder the question of where to seek that infinite value that humanity is pursuing. 

But what should one do when they cannot solve such a problem no matter how much they think about it? How much anguish will they endure in fighting against such thoughts? They may think, but because they cannot find a solution, or because their thoughts do not align with reality, they find themselves in a pitiable position. However, if they can stand before their stagnant state with new hope and a new direction, and boldly declare before America and the world, "This is the path that everyone must take," how wonderful would that be? At that moment, the teacher had such thoughts about that person.

When we consider these issues, we can understand that humanity today needs a liberation akin to a second or third liberation. 

When we look towards the northwest today, we see the communist regimes of the Soviet Union and China. Nearly a billion people are living in bondage there. Are they living freely and happily? It is just talk; in reality, that is not the case. Even in the democratic world we call the free world, we cannot say that we are free, let alone in the dictatorial communist world. It is undoubtedly a fact that they are even less free.

From this perspective, if the democratic world today demands a third liberation, wouldn’t the communist world demand a second liberation? When we look at this issue, where will the new ideologies and philosophies that can become the vanguard of the second and third liberations come from? They cannot emerge from the human world. Humanity has struggled for thousands of years to achieve this liberation, but has not been able to create the necessary environment or content. Therefore, liberation cannot be centered solely on humanity.

Then, who should be the center? Who should be the focus if not humanity? It must be God. Therefore, if God exists, that is fortunate, but if God does not exist, it is despair.

If a politician, a great sage, or a prominent figure attempts to advocate a new ideology and philosophy to guide humanity, they must bring in some imaginary absolute power to help those who are in a state of despair, for human strength alone is insufficient. In other words, even if there is no God, we must not leave humanity in an environment of despair and bondage; it is time for the intervention of some absolute being to liberate humanity from such conditions. Even if there is no God, by establishing an imaginary God, those who look to that God will move towards a heavenly realm, approaching a better and more original place.

Thus, we must recognize the approaching time when we should advocate for an imaginary God, even if there is no real God. How wonderful would it be to be someone who is certain that God exists during such times? Then, wouldn’t we have to take responsibility and shout with all our might before the world? This is the issue.

Establishing a relationship with God is of utmost importance.

What will the Unification Church do in front of the world that is groaning at the limits of despair? What the Unification Church must present before humanity is the question of whether God exists. We must address the issue of whether God truly exists or not. This is the problem.

Some of you may be worried that you cannot find the path of purpose through your own strength, but what is more pressing than that? Do I truly know God? Have I decisively realized that God exists? Do I truly know the one who governs my entire life, who has power over life and death and everything? This is the most important issue.

God knows not only the life we have lived from the past but also our present selves and our future destinies. However, because humans are ignorant, they do not follow the path of the highest destiny they should take. Some people have a predetermined fate, but they do not follow that path, and there are blessings they could enjoy, yet they do not fully enjoy them and instead are surrounded by an environment of despair that leads to their own destruction. We often see such occurrences around us.

Therefore, if there is an absolute being who knows all the fates surrounding us and can guide our destinies in a better direction, then knowing that being and establishing a relationship with them is of utmost importance.

We, who have inherited the fallen lineage from our ancestors, have bloodlines that carry the legacy of their fall. Thus, we often find ourselves bound by such concepts in our daily lives and customs, which can lead us to confine all our hopes. Furthermore, deep down, we may cry out, "I should not be like this," urging ourselves to overcome our circumstances and move forward anew, yet we remain unable to escape from those environments and abandon our habits.

What prevents us from overcoming such habitual tendencies? It is because our living environments bind us. Within these living environments, not only personal issues but also racial issues, relationships between the rich and the poor, and marital relationships are intertwined.

When we look at these issues, we can see that the habits inherited historically and the living environment itself become factors that obstruct and negate the very center of the second hope that is meant to stir our inner selves and awaken a new self. Our lives, habits, and historical traditions are like that.

Therefore, how we can break free from such habits is our task. Historical figures and saints have fought with their lives over the question of whether they could escape the environments that bound and surrounded them and move forward based on a worldview and lifestyle centered on the future. We know that such people are saints and martyrs. They fought for the liberation of history, sacrificing their lives to overcome all the evil habits and environments of history.

When we look at these historical figures, we realize that we today are unable to escape our living environments, and thus we need a second and third liberation. Therefore, we must make an inner decision to break free from our current positions.

Making that decision is difficult with one’s own strength alone. Even when we look at the history of a nation, there have been numerous patriots and great figures, but what they have left behind is only the reality of today. Therefore, we must be prepared for greater strength and greater sacrifice than they made. Without that, we cannot overcome this reality, and it is difficult to make resolutions and decisions with our own strength alone. Self-reflection and inner determination are not enough.

To purify such a society and this earth and to become a person capable of revolutionizing it, one must have more than just a resolution that stirs their own heart. That is why the power of God is needed. Even if one dies a million times, they must have a strong resolution to completely abandon their own environment and habits. However, that is not easy. Thus, we need a source of power that can stimulate us a hundredfold or a thousandfold.

Such power cannot be gained through historical figures who have come and gone. Therefore, if there is a God who can supply me with power greater than that power and stimulate me through that power, and if there is someone who knows that God, then a new history will begin from that person.

So, do Unification Church members truly know God in the true sense? They do not. That is the problem. What is more important than my relationship with this era and this world? It is my relationship with God. Therefore, you must clearly understand this era and the world, and before concluding that "this world will perish," you need to have a realization that allows you to resolve that you will not suffer in this world.

This realization is not something that can be gained through any knowledge of historical eras. It is a realization gained from a new perspective. It is not something that can be obtained through humanity that has passed through history. It is only possible through a third power. There is no other way to seek such a path. That path can only be prepared by God.

In such a serious situation, God, whom we must seek even if it means giving up history and the world, is the God we must find at all costs, no matter what effort, struggle, pain, or injustice we endure. A person who seeks that God is a strong person. They cannot be changed by anything in society or any ideology in the world. They will start from a conscious position that has the subjectivity to push forward against the trends of their environment and the world.

How can we bring forth a new emergence of a conscious self that can step forward with a power and resolution that surpasses everything in this world? This is an important issue that the world needs at this point in time.

The assurance of God is the solution to the problem.

From this perspective, questioning whether God exists or not is not the issue. That does not provide a solution to the problem. We cannot engage in debates over whether God exists or not. When we are certain that "God exists! He definitely exists!" that is where the solution begins. We must say, "Because God truly exists, we must act accordingly," in order to truly embrace liberation. This must apply not only to me but also to others.

The hardships of our social environment are not just personal hardships. They apply to me, to you, to our nation, to other nations, and to all humanity.

Therefore, each person has a desire to break through and transcend this environment. Thus, if a solution is established that can overcome and transcend this environment, saying, "This is how it is," then the world can turn towards that one place at once.

In this regard, God does not push humanity into tragedy and despair to sacrifice them forever in a world of darkness. When He provides a bright light like a lighthouse in this pitch-black world, it is to present a direction for humanity, allowing those who have been crying out in the realm of darkness to rush towards God with shouts of joy, forming a new trend at the end of the century. This is what we must consider.

What is needed here is a conscious individual, family, tribe, and nation that can say, "This is what God is like." When a nation that can connect in this way appears, the world will have no choice but to look up to that nation.

What the Unification Church advocates is not the question of whether God exists or not. It is not even a matter of "He will exist." Yet, because we have not yet found the turning point for resolving that issue, we are still in conflict. Our assertion is that God exists. God undoubtedly exists. Before any explanation, we affirm that God undoubtedly exists.

What is God doing?

Then, what is God doing? He is working to embrace and revive the world. His efforts are not only for the world but also for "me." Realizing this is more precious than anything else in the world. What does that make everyone? Thus, the issue is the recognition of God. God undoubtedly exists.

What is heaven? The Unification Church does not speak of a heaven of faith. It speaks of righteousness. It speaks of being saved through service. Can you serve without knowing? Knowing what is taught in the Unification Church is not the issue. When taught, anyone can come to know. However, even among Unification Church members, there are those who are unsure whether God exists or not.

How many times a day do you realize that God exists? How often do you feel that God exists within 24 hours? Can those who claim they will be saved through service do so by serving for just one or two hours in a day? God is more urgently needed than air. God is more urgently needed than water. God is more precious than food. But do you feel that way?

The turning point of liberation.
You need to understand why Christianity is declining. The early Christians knew God. Read the Book of Acts. Whenever they went somewhere, they did so based on God's revelation. No one sought their own path in every action they took. They moved by connecting every issue with God.

But why did this early Christianity, which could bear fruit due to its roots, decline in the Middle Ages? For them, God remained only in their heads. The God they believed in was only a God of thought. He was not a factual God. That is why it became a problem. The God of thought was not a God for the world, but a God for themselves. That is why they had to perish. Thus, they are now in a condition where they need to be liberated again.

They are among those who need liberation, and they must be the first to be liberated. They are the most pitiful. They claim to have sought God, yet they do not know the certain conviction of God, they participate in God's work, act on behalf of God, and stand in God's glorious position while selling God centered around themselves. They must be judged first. You need to understand this fact. Hypocrisy is unnecessary for those who do not know God. The Antichrist is also unnecessary for those who do not know God. The problem lies with those who claim to know God. Therefore, you must be certain whether God exists or not. This is the issue.

Then, what is the starting point of liberation and our responsibility? It is God. Does God exist or not? If He exists, how does He exist? If He exists as a parent, where is He? What is the relationship between God and me? These are the issues.

This relationship is currently twisted, tangled, and complicated. Why is that? Because the motivations are different. The new solution that can correct this is not found in human history, but in a place that transcends history. Therefore, we must start not from the place where religion has introduced God throughout history, but leap beyond that.

From this perspective, the Unification Church is necessary. Looking at the current global situation, the world has reached a dismal final cliff. Now we are at a point where we must either break our heads against that cliff or break the cliff itself. We have entered a time when no one can save the world with their own power.

Let us recall our liberation on August 15th. In some ways, it might have been better if that day of liberation had never come. If our lives under Japanese rule had simply continued, we might have retained the fighting spirit of a united nation to struggle for a day of liberation. However, today, with democracy and various ideologies, we have all scattered and lost even our national spirit, making our liberation at that time almost meaningless.

The liberation we desire is not centered around South Korea, the current Republic of Korea. We hoped for a liberation that unites the North and South. 

Considering the current situation in the Republic of Korea, is it better than the Japanese colonial era? It is not. Why? Because the 38th parallel was created. The issues of democracy and communism are tied to this 38th parallel, so without resolving the global stage, there is no way for the North and South to unite. Liberation from the oppression of Japan could occur if the emperor of a single nation surrendered. However, currently, liberation cannot be achieved merely through the claims of one nation, and we must recognize that the current Republic of Korea is in a more pitiful position than during the oppression of Japanese rule.

Think about it. Do you think China will retreat and the Soviet Union will retreat? As long as the Soviet Union and China remain, North Korea will also remain. They are all communist countries. Communism is materialism, and democracy is idealism. Because the world is divided and fighting over this materialism and idealism, we cannot end the struggle between these two ideologies without resolving their philosophical foundations.

So how can we solve this problem? It cannot be done with just any theory. A person must emerge who can say, "God is with me." And on the day when they teach, "This is what God wants for all people," both materialism and idealism will yield.

If God exists, such a day must inevitably come. If God's will is clearly revealed before the materialistic thought that denies God, communism will crumble. When we clearly understand that this is God's will in today's chaotic democratic world, it will disappear.

If you know that God exists...

What was the factor that allowed the people of the Eastern United States to pioneer the West long ago? It was the political propaganda of the politicians of that time. They claimed that there were mountains of gold in the West and that everything was rich, and that it belonged to those who went there first. So, not knowing whether they would live or die, they saw their companions die and still thought, "Let's go a little further, just a little further," and thus pioneered the West. They believed the rumors were true, and even if everyone died, they were fueled by the hope that they would become the richest person in the world if they survived.

People are like that. When a miner sets out to find a vein and is exhausted to the point of death, if he hears that if he digs ten more times, he will surely find a rich vein, what would he do? Would you keep digging or not? Even if it means risking death, he would keep going. Therefore, where is the problem? It lies with you.

The way Abel restores Cain.

The standard of liberation
