Experiences in Seodaemun Prison
Suddenly, people who do not know this teacher come and take him away to imprison him. They say, "What about the Son of God?" and throw him in with murderers and robbers. They tell him to be a servant. At that time, one must serve. Do you understand?

To subdue murderers and robbers, I must first submit. Submitting 100 percent first is heaven. If I submit 1000 percent, then 900 percent of the murderers will naturally submit to me. That is why, even in prison, the teacher became the master of the murderers without speaking and became their mother and father. They do not hide their secrets from me; they tell me everything. When the teacher was about to leave prison, even the most wicked person there shed tears, saying he wished the teacher would not leave. That is how it was made.

This is the path the teacher has walked until now.
When I entered Seodaemun Prison, the head of the detention center took the newcomers to stamp their documents. I will never forget that head. I have forgotten his name now, but at that time, he looked at me and laughed, saying, "The Unification Church is like this, huh?" My feelings were quite bad, and I told him to shut up because it was noisy, and I thought that when I left here, I would definitely make the detectives, guards, and even the warden submit to me. But would I evangelize there? However, after a few days, they came to me in the morning and said, "Did you sleep well?" Who would greet me just because someone told them to?

Sometimes, if I just stay still, they come in the morning and just pass by. I think, "You should come back after passing by," and sure enough, they turn back. Then they come and go again. When I think, "You should come back and greet me," they do that again. One day, they came to talk to me, and one morning, I was eating rice cake, but it got stuck in my throat and wouldn’t go down. Why wouldn’t the rice cake go down? It is because the ancestors are blocking it. They know that if their ancestors treat the teacher poorly, it will be a big problem. So that is how it is. They secretly ate rice cake and got scolded. I already know such things. So when I tell them about it, they call me "Master." I know their weaknesses. After that, they served the teacher well. That is how it became.

By the time I was about to leave, even the chief came to me, bringing summer melons and watermelons. He said things that he couldn’t even say to his brothers. He talked about the experiences he had while witnessing to the teacher for a few months. So, would I evangelize him because I want to receive a witness? Even without the teacher evangelizing, he could be evangelized. I told you that when I was in prison, even if I kept my mouth shut, I was directly evangelized in the spiritual world, right? Park Jeong-hwa was also someone who was evangelized in that way.

Thus, we all must become holy sons and daughters who can call upon the precious name of the Father, serve the Father, and shed sweat and blood for Him, so we earnestly ask for Your permission.  
Wherever our sweat and tears fall, we know that the unbreakable bond with the Father is intertwined, and the fruits of Your labor that have emerged on the foundation of restoration will be borne. The tears we shed will become the tears of the earth in place of the tears You shed, and the blood we shed will become the blood of the earth in place of the blood You shed.  
We have understood that since the day we entered the path of the Father’s suffering, we cannot uproot this without going through the process of suffering. We have seen the history of the first Israel, which could not avoid the bloody struggles throughout the 4,000 years of history because the Father’s will is to bear fruit from the place where it began. We know that this will of the Father could not avoid the altar of bloody martyrdom as Christianity emerged through the second Israel to the third Israel.  
Thus, we must once again realize what position we stand in before Your holy will, which has chosen the Korean Peninsula as the center of the third Israel, which is centered on spirit and body.  
Now, even if one is in their teens, twenties, thirties, or forties, they must realize that their current self is not the same as the self that existed in the past historical process, but rather the self that is through all the examples of the Father who governs the providence of restoration throughout human history.  
Even if one’s self is extremely small and insignificant, when we think that something great can start from that insignificant place, and that the core of the whole can be determined from such a tiny place, we must clearly realize that we came from the Father, we were left by the Father, and now we must walk with the Father.  
Thus, we earnestly hope and desire that there will be a decisive place in our hearts and bodies, or in some corner of our environment, or at some time, where we can say that Your unique son and daughter have come here and can discuss and make promises with the Father.  
Until now, we have called upon the Father a thousand or ten thousand times. We must not call upon the Father as if it were a habit or a mere formality. When we call out "Father!" we must feel the boiling blood surging from our marrow and experience the unity of our cells aligning with the heart of the Father, so we earnestly ask for Your permission to become such conscious beings.  
When we feel the sorrowful heart that the Father felt, we must be sons and daughters who realize that it is a sorrow that cannot be blocked by our own senses. When we are filled with joy in contact with the Father, we must be able to elevate ourselves in a glorious manner that cannot be exchanged for anything on this earth and reveal the authority of being Your sons.  
Father, whenever I think of Your amazing will to make us, who seem ugly in Your sight, whiter than white and purer than pure, and to equip us with the authority of heavenly princes and princesses, I cannot help but feel a profound and boundless heart, and I cannot call upon You without tears. I earnestly hope and desire that the sons and daughters here will deeply feel this.  
During this 40-day summer pioneering evangelism period, please remember Your beloved children who are struggling in the local areas. If the amount of sweat and tears they shed has not yet reached its fullness, please let us realize that the responsibility to push them again to fill it lies with the Unification Church. Also, I earnestly hope and desire that we will clearly understand that the future of the Unification Church is something I must be responsible for and we must be responsible for.  
Since You are the one who started this, we know that You are also the one who must reap the results. Even if the process takes ten years, twenty years, or even a lifetime, or if it takes three times, ten times, or thirty times longer, we must be able to recognize that the path You are on is the right path, and we earnestly ask and desire to become sons and daughters who can comply and follow the heavenly will.  
Today, when we think of 'liberation and our responsibility,' we realize that You are both the driving force of liberation and the very essence of liberation. Therefore, every time the pulse of the arteries beats with the blood that flows from Your heart, may our pulses beat as well, and every time the power absorbed into the veins collides, may we be drawn closer to You.  
When You move, we must also move, and when You are still, we must also be still. When You are joyful, we must also be joyful, and when You are sorrowful, we must also be sons and daughters who share in that sorrow.  
As we head towards the nation of peace and the kingdom of peace, may the hopeful sons and daughters take on a dignified and vibrant posture, and may we not become those who are stimulated by defeat in the face of evil forces. We earnestly hope and desire to become heavenly warriors who can punish this for ten million years with heavenly authority and to become heavenly soldiers.  
We know that You, Father, gathered the devastated Israelite nation that had fallen in the wilderness centered on Joshua and Caleb and led them towards the hopeful kingdom of the second Canaan, and we are aware of the words You commanded to Joshua and Caleb to "be strong and courageous." (The rest is not recorded.)  
**The Master of History and the World**  
The title of what I want to share with you today is 'The Master of History and the World.'  
You gathered here are young boys and girls, and the title seems too grand for you, so I wonder if everyone can understand it well.  
It seems that about 400 people have gathered here today, and many of you may be seeing the teacher for the first time. If there are those seeing the teacher for the first time, please raise your hands. There are quite a few... you can put them down. Now, how about those who have been in the Unification Church for less than six months? Please raise your hands. You can put them down. And how about those who have been here for more than three years? You can put them down. How about those who have been here for more than a year? Please raise your hands. You can put them down. How about those who have been here for less than a year? It seems to be about half of you. I understand.  
The reason I ask this is that it is important to know what kind of faith experience you all have. Also, knowing this allows me to give you appropriate teachings.  
Do you know why the youth period is so good?  
Your youth, like yours, is a wonderful time. Why is it good? Because during your time, you want to boast about everything. Please raise your hands if you are middle school students.  
This is the time when you want to boast the most. Even if there is just a little good thing at home, you want to brag about it. Adults worry about rumors if they boast about good things, but during youth, if something good happens at home, you want to brag about it on the tram, on the bus, or anywhere. Thus, during youth, it is a time when you like to boast and hope to have something substantial to boast about.  
That is why mothers and fathers also hope for good parents. When they become good parents, it is exciting. Also, even when looking at their home, there are families where five members are crammed into a small room, with parents and siblings sleeping in awkward positions. Such children wish their home was better than others. So, if their home is a bit better than others, they boast about having such a home.  
And among siblings, if there is a brother studying abroad in the United States or Japan, they want to brag about that brother. If there is an older brother who has become a doctor, they say, "My brother is Dr. So-and-so."  
This youth period is good because when something good is in your heart, you want to reveal it as it is and make it your own in the world. The desire to boast about good things indicates a strong absorption capacity to make anything good their own. Do you understand what that means?  
Have the desire to be the best in the world.  
Not long ago, our South Korean soccer players went to Indonesia and won a championship trophy, right? When you watch such soccer matches, they are really exciting. So, you want to become a soccer player too. When you watch a boxing match and see a boxer bleeding in the ring, you might think about how you want to be that champion wearing the championship belt after defeating your opponent amidst the cheers of the audience. Is that right?  
Also, when you see a marathon runner, you might think about how you want to quit the hard part and just be that runner.  
And when the president comes out to give a New Year’s address, it looks impressive. Just think about how all the people tune in to the radio or television and listen carefully. How does that make you feel? You might want to be the president at least once, right?  
Seeing such people makes you want to become like them, and seeing other people makes you want to become like them too. In our country, everyone wants to make the best of everything their own. Is that true for you? "Yes." If not, then you might as well die. (Laughter) That's how it is.  
Then, have you ever felt, "I can’t stand being in Seoul; Namsan is blocking my view, and I can’t bear it"? Have you ever thought about how nice it would be to see all the way to the White House in the United States? Have you ever thought, "I can’t stand being in Seoul; Namsan, fly away! Inwangsan, fly away! Bukaksan, fly away! After everything flies away, I want to see what’s at the end that I want to see"? You should think about such things.  
When you go to the beach, have you ever thought, "I want to drink all this seawater or see what’s at the bottom of the sea and make the good things there my own"? Have you thought about that, or not? "I haven’t." If you haven’t thought about that, it’s a bit unpleasant, isn’t it? (Laughter) If that’s the case, then you are not even the sons and daughters of South Korea. You cannot be someone who can provide any benefits for the future of South Korea.  
When a nice airplane flies by, you should be able to say, "I may be like this now, but that pilot is me." And even though the pilot flying the plane is doing well, you should have the mindset that "I will be better than that." There should be people who think like that while eating. Many of you might want to become such a person. So, there are many people who resolve to say, "I will make the best in the world my own," "I will do something great." Do you want to do that, or not?  
Until now, you may not have been able to do that, but from now on, how many of you want to do that?  
How much can you do starting from now with the teachings you have received? There might be someone here who is twenty years old; when will they catch up? It may be that you have not been able to do so since birth. If someone has been like that since birth, no matter how hard I try, I cannot win a world-class medal.  
To possess the best in the world,  
So what is the best in the world in your hearts? This is the question. If there is something that is the best in the world, our young boys and girls must seize it. If one person is not enough, then ten, a hundred, a thousand, or even ten thousand people must come together to seize it.  
How many middle and high school students are there in South Korea? Is it about several million? There are many groups. If about a hundred thousand people swarm like ants, we can seize something good. Can you mobilize a hundred thousand people? If you can, then we must engage in a movement to mobilize people and seize it, right? "We must."  
But the only person who knows that is me. I need to mobilize you, but what will you do? If you do not mobilize, the best in the world will forever have nothing to do with you.  
However, if you say, "I will mobilize a hundred thousand people within a few years," and step forward voluntarily, you will make the best in the world your own.  
In other words, if all the youth, middle, and high school students in countless countries around the world are pushed aside and our country’s students take the lead, our country will become the champion nation for middle and high school students in the world. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Wouldn’t you feel that way? You might not know that feeling, but if you did, would you do it? "I will." Do you want to do it or not? "I will." For young people, it should be stimulating to ask, "Do you want to do it or not?" (Laughter) Some of you who are seeing the teacher for the first time might think, "I thought our teacher was a dignified and wonderful person, but I didn’t expect this." But being dignified is not exciting.
It’s exciting to ask, “Do you want to do it or not?” The teacher must understand this well in order to guide you. Do you want to try it or not? “I want to try.” However, even in that desire to try, there are about 400 steps. You have answered, but that doesn’t mean they are all the same. Analyzing it reveals that there are about 400 steps. But when you truly want to do it, how many steps are there? Just one step. Do you really want to do it? “Yes.” How much do you want to do it? Would you do it even if one arm is cut off or one leg is severed? After that, if your left leg and left arm are cut off, or if your right leg and right arm are completely severed, can you still be happy and not care about losing them? If there is something you would do even if it costs you your neck, would you do it or not? “I would.” You are saying you would do it while feeling a chill in your stomach, right? (Laughter) It’s easy to say. Saying “I will” comes out quickly, but actions take a million times longer. Therefore, the most important issue is whether you are prepared to invest your hands and feet, and eventually your life. When 500,000 or a million people can be mobilized to do that, it is an indescribable, tremendous power. A power that cannot be expressed in words is scarier than absolute power. When that tremendous power explodes, what could be scary if a million people say they will put their necks on the line? Would you be afraid of the Communist Party? They would not be scary anymore. Do you understand?

What should we be proud of?
Now you are wearing glasses. Whether they are binoculars or blue-tinted glasses, all 400 of you are wearing glasses. If you are in the third year of high school, you are around 18 years old, right? Then some female students will soon turn 20, and after a few years, it will be time to get married, so there will be those who are preparing to get married. Isn’t that so? As I said earlier, the younger generation is full of a desire to boast about anything, and if you are going to boast, you want to hold on to the best in the world, right? Isn’t that true? “Yes.” Then what is that? Is it the President of the United States? “No.” If not that, then what? “The return of the Lord.” The return of the Lord? “Yes.” Who taught you that? Did you learn it, or did it come from your heart? Do you truly want to boast that it is the best? Can you boast that our teacher is the best person in South Korea and scold those who oppose you by saying, “This is not a lie, it is a fact”? Can you fight with them? “I can.” If you have the best thing, what is it? Our young ladies, would you like to boast about being born as the daughter of a wealthy family and taking a diamond ring worth several carats when you get married? Is that the best thing? Would you boast if your house is one of the biggest in Seoul, second or third, or even the first? Such things are all trivial. Once dissatisfaction arises, everything disappears. In an instant, it all burns away and disappears.

So what do you really want to boast about? This is the desire that young people have. If your school principal is excellent, you want to boast about that principal, right? However, no matter how excellent the principal is, when they reach about 70 or 80 years old, they will become frail. No matter how strong they are, they cannot avoid aging. In the end, they will disappear.

Then what is the best? Is it a lump of gold? If you eat a lump of gold, will you be full? When you are starving to death, will you take a gold lump the size of a mountain? At that time, you would want to trade a mountain-sized lump of gold for a bowl of rice. Wouldn’t you? “Yes.” At that time, a lump of gold is nothing.

Why am I saying this? Because I have experienced such things when I was young. Growing up in the countryside, I felt frustrated. I wanted to see everything by going around in circles (gesturing). I couldn’t help but think, “What is truly good?” I lived with all sorts of thoughts.

So what is the best in the world? Please tell me. What is the best? “Truth.” If it is truth, there is truth among truths. “New truth.” The new truth is the same. When spring comes, we say it’s new leaves, right? The mulberry tree has new leaves, the willow has new leaves, the pine tree has new leaves; all have new leaves. So what does truth do? Does truth eat? Will you be full if you eat it? (Laughter) What do you do when you know the truth? After graduating from college and becoming a Ph.D., what will you do? “I will use it.” Where will you use it? The truth must be a truth that can be used in the world. It should not be something that can only be used for a time but a truth that can be used forever. This is why it becomes a problem.

Then can you be happy with only truth? If there is a king of male truth in the world, can you claim to be the best with just that? There must be a queen of female truth. If there is a king of male truth, what else must there be? “A queen of female truth.” Then if the queen of female truth stands firm and claims, “I am the best in the world,” what happens? At that time, both men and women will set aside truth, and what can come next as a result? Love. This is how it becomes. Isn’t that right? Love will be the issue.

Then what kind of love is that? The love of a younger sibling for an older brother is necessary, and love for one’s country is also necessary. Additionally, love between countries is needed.

If you are going to be, you must be first.
Then what kind of person is a truly loving person? If an older brother loves me, is that love enough just to love me? It cannot end there. The older brother must love the younger sibling with a love that all humanity seeks. Do you truly love your older brother as a younger sibling? Have you thought about whether that love represents history and the world?

If you have thought about it, how many points does that love have? How many points is it for the older brother to love me? Is it zero points? Ten points? Or is it 20, 50, 70, or 100 points? Is there anything above 100 points? If you add more than 100 points, then it exists.

Do you want to score 100 points, or do you want to score 120 points? Don’t you all want to score 120 points? There can be 120 points. When I was in school, I scored up to 105 points. (Laughter) How did I score 105 points? At that time, even the homeroom teacher was impressed. Is there any judgment or trial for scoring 105 points? The fact that there isn’t means it can happen. So I am curious about how many points your love has. Isn’t that right? “Yes.”

Don’t you want to know how your parents rank in South Korea? When you think about where your parents rank, it might be second or third, but if they are not first, it feels bad. The son’s heart wishes for a mother who is first among mothers, who dresses up and dances. Have you thought about such a standard of a mother? “I haven’t.” That’s why you have lived pitifully until now.

People need love. You feel sorry for orphans who do not receive parental or sibling love. These people do not know parental love and sibling love. No matter how much you explain parental love and sibling love to them, they cannot respond with “That’s right.” It’s like a mute who has eaten honey. Honey is sweet, but they cannot explain it. Therefore, love is not created alone. It occurs among sons and daughters centered around parents.

There are patriots centered around South Korea. We call people like Yu Gwan-sun or Admiral Yi Sun-sin loyal martyrs, but have you thought about how many points they have? How many points do those people have? Also, what rank does South Korea hold in the world? If South Korea is not first in the world, it doesn’t matter how loudly you shout that it is first; it is useless. If it is not first in the world, it feels bad. Have you thought about that? If you are going to be, you must be first.

What kind of person you will be depends on your determination.
From this perspective, are Admiral Yi Sun-sin and Yu Gwan-sun, whom we admire as loyal martyrs, loyal to the Japanese people as well? To the Japanese, they are arch-enemies. So it feels bad. If you take a boat for seven or eight hours across the Tsushima Strait and arrive in Japan, and they say they are loyal martyrs, they would want to cut off your head. Isn’t that right? Would that make you feel good or bad? “Bad.”

If the Asian era arrives and all of Asia becomes like one country, can we say we should follow the traditions of Admiral Yi Sun-sin and Yu Gwan-sun? Do you think saying, “I have come instead of Yu Gwan-sun” or “I have come instead of Admiral Yi Sun-sin” would resonate? Do you think it would resonate? “No, it wouldn’t.” It would not resonate. Similarly, a loyal person from Japan can become an enemy of our country. A loyal person from China can also become an enemy of our country.

From this standpoint, is there anyone among the Japanese who can truly become my friend? Is there anyone who can receive all my love? There is no one who can pass this test. Isn’t that right? Therefore, from now on, depending on your determination as young people, all sorts of people will appear.

Did the teacher have a time like yours? “Yes.” I did not. I might have looked similar, but my thoughts were different. I was absurd. Even when my mother gave me apples or melons, I would ask her, “Where did this melon come from?” Then my mother would say, “Where did it come from? Your older brother bought it.” Then I would ask, “From which field did he buy it? Did Grandma pick it, or did Uncle pick it, or did someone older than my brother pick it, or did someone older than my sister pick it?” I was very curious about that. I would only eat melons that I could boast about; I wouldn’t know if the melon was stolen. If I didn’t know for sure, I would feel bad eating it. I would rather starve to death than eat that.

Be a person who helps others.
When I think about it this way, what is the best? What is the best in South Korea? To you, your parents are the best, right? It’s good because you depend on your parents. And your school teachers are good because they teach you. Isn’t that right? The people you say are good are those who add value to you. Your attention is focused only on those who add value to you. This is the nature of youth. That’s why it’s good to depend on your parents, but if they make you a little unhappy, you cry and complain, “Why do you only love my sister and brother and treat me like this?” When you come home from school and are asked to do the dishes, you make a fuss. (Laughter) In any case, you only like conditions that are positive for you.

Even at school, if the teacher looks at you with wide eyes and says something unpleasant, you dislike it, and even if you have done something wrong, you prefer a teacher who pats you on the back and forgives you, saying, “Don’t do that next time.” You are in that phase right now. You also complain if there is even a little blood on your fingernails, saying, “Oh, my hand!” You are in that phase, right? “Yes.” You like to seek out people you can depend on.

When you observe the world, is there anyone you can depend on forever? Is there someone who wants to take from me or make me dependent on them? History wants to take from me. That’s why conflicts arise. Therefore, doing good deeds is extremely difficult.

Is a person who only likes what adds value to them a good person or a bad person? Such a person generally falls into the category of bad people. Is a person who wishes only for their own good while others suffer a good person? That person is a bad person. However, in youth, that can be forgiven. You must understand that.

However, if you reach your 20s and 30s and still try to take only what adds value to you in all aspects of society, that person will become an enemy and will be rejected not only at work but everywhere. At that time, you must be someone who adds value to others to be liked. Thus, youth and adulthood are different. You must understand this.

Can what you think is good now be good forever? Can the parents you think are good now cultivate a character that will be good forever, and can the teachers you think are good now become lifelong mentors? Even if that is not the case, a person who can boast that they have the generosity and wealth to give forever because they have received a legacy cannot help but be a filial child in front of their parents and a necessary person for their country.

If you owe a debt, you must repay it. Receiving parental love is also to repay it, and hoping to benefit from your teacher’s love is also to repay it. You must not forget that.

However, everything you wish for now is easy to think of from your own perspective. Your generation is particularly so. It is easy to think centered around your home or your country.

Thoughts that boys and girls should have.
If there is a teenager among you who thinks, “My parents may not love me greatly, but they are wonderful people. They don’t show love or do what other parents do, but my parents are better than anyone else,” that person is excellent. Do you understand what I mean?

When you think about how many people are without parents, you might think, “What if I had been one of those people? The fact that my parents are still alive is precious to me. Just seeing them makes me happy.” Such a person can be considered a filial child.

While studying at school, many people want to study but cannot. When you see this reality in Korea and think, “Even though I might not have the fortune to meet that teacher, the fact that I have met them, regardless of their love, is for my study, and the meeting is for the teacher to teach me,” how precious is that position? If you understand that and study, will you fail? Would someone who thinks like that fail? Absolutely not. However, among students who argue with teachers and complain, many fail.
Wait and see. 
Regarding the country, no matter how miserable and ugly the Republic of Korea may be, how grateful is it that I was born as one of its citizens? How many countries are still suffering under the oppression of other nations, fighting desperately to reclaim their sovereignty, and enduring hardships under the hooves of oppression? When I think of such countries, I should truly be grateful for my own. If I love this land more than anyone else, fearing that it might be taken away, and if I love this nation even more, then that country will not perish even if it is destined to fail. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 
If a king or a sovereign considers serving their country as the greatest honor of their life and feels fulfilled by it, then that society will inevitably become united. When this happens, the world will change in an instant. What causes this change? It depends on our thoughts. 
How should a person live? 
Where do good people and bad people part ways? They are involved in the same event, but one follows the path of goodness while the other is led astray. Even among siblings born of the same parents, some resent their parents and separate from them, while others, even if they do not receive their parents' love, possess the heart to love their parents. Those who have such a heart can receive even the hidden love of their parents. Such a person becomes a filial child. 
The same applies to a nation. If one dedicates their life to loving their country, day and night, and influences the entire environment in which they live with that love, then that person cannot help but be called a loyal subject. 
Therefore, how should a person live? They should think of those who are in positions lower and worse than their own. Moreover, if they encounter someone in a more difficult situation, they should feel compassion for that person and be grateful for their own circumstances. Not only gratitude, but when they help others, they become someone who is welcomed not only in their own country but also in others. 
When we look at the history of loyal subjects and saints today, there are not many who became saints or loyal subjects while living well as the children of wealthy families. Even in times of chaos and despair, when the nation or society is in turmoil, they took pride in being born in that country and having parents. They loved their country and parents more than anyone else, striving to help those who were more unfortunate than themselves. When they unite with such a heart and pave a better path, problems will be resolved. Such history starts from the love of one’s country, the love of one’s parents, and the love of one’s teachers. From there, a new history spreads horizontally beyond nations to the world. It is through such people that history has developed. 
If a wealthy person does not know how to be grateful for their wealth and only strives to accumulate more money, they will eventually fail. A person who thinks, "I have earned enough," and feels great gratitude toward their country and people, with the desire to help, can become even wealthier. A person who, despite being wealthy, cannot feel gratitude and is only greedy will ultimately fall into the pit they have dug for themselves. Isn’t that true? "Yes." 
What does a needle thief become? "A cow thief." You know that well. 
The issue is how to digest the trials that come our way. 
So, who are the masters of history and the world? The masters of history and the world are one. If such a person is needed in the Republic of Korea, what kind of person will become the master of Korea? If there is a nation that is more miserable than ours, and one cannot love that nation and its people, then a person who feels the misery of that nation while deciding to love their own country even more will inevitably advance. God desires such people. 
Everyone, when we look at the saints, they are just like you. They were born from their mothers' wombs and grew up drinking milk, just like everyone else. But what is different about them? There may be some among you who were born in the Republic of Korea but resent being born here. Can such a person become the master of Korea? Such a person can never be a master. 
I heard that there are people who walked dozens or hundreds of miles to get here. Among you, there may be someone who thinks, "I came to the Unification Church, but what is this about restoration and walking distances longer than a thousand miles? This is ridiculous; oh, my fate! My legs hurt, and I have blisters on my feet, limping around. What should I do? I can’t back out now since I’ve made a name for myself." If someone has such thoughts, they would have been better off not coming. Even if blisters form on their feet and they are in pain, they should be able to say, "Thank you." Throughout history, how many people have disappeared in search of their country and true life, even in prison-like conditions? When I think of those who paved the way for me, I should walk with joy. If someone walks this path while sympathizing with those people and shedding tears, they become friends of the righteous who have come and gone in the past. That is what is wonderful. 
How many have entered prison, endured beatings, and faced life-and-death situations for the sake of this path? Not just themselves, but entire families or organizations have sacrificed while walking this path. When I think of that, I should be able to say, "Thank you," even for being in such a position. If one can do that, they will go to heaven even if they do not want to. 
So, as you move forward with your aspirations, the question is how you will digest all the trials that come your way. If someone finds themselves in such a situation and thinks, "I must be above the standards I enjoyed in the world until now; if I fall below that, I cannot do it," they will fail. The higher the mountain, the deeper the valley. If one falls from the peak of such a mountain into a deep valley, they will be shattered. Walking this path can often leave one feeling dizzy. 
That is why you should think, "Today is just one scene of trial. What scene will unfold tomorrow?" Therefore, you must lay down a solid bridge to reach the true place. No matter how dizzy you feel, you must be thorough and say, "The path I am taking is clear in all directions. I will not be invaded." 
From that position, you must make friends with history and consult with the times. You must not become a person who complains and grumbles. Even loyal subjects and martyrs of a nation have often disappeared in prisons, suffering hardships. However, those who die loving their enemies without resenting them can feel the greatest liberation, even if they are in prison. That is what I believe. 
What does this come from? It comes from humanity. You must have the desire to love beyond yourself, to sympathize beyond yourself, to help beyond yourself, to relate beyond yourself, and to want to live with others. 
A person who lives for the world is the master of the world. 
Today, young people have the foundation to like everything. However, the thought that "I must like more" should be removed. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." What is good depends on our thoughts. True goodness must be eternal. Goodness that is centered on oneself is not absolute. Goodness connects to the generations that follow.

Teachings of the Saints 
The sages were of that kind. Confucius was a person from the state of Lu during the Spring and Autumn period thousands of years ago, but he did not just think of a few countries. Even when looking at the difficult environment he was born into and the chaotic society, he did not complain. He sought the true path he could help others with, even without siblings, with a grateful heart centered on his parents. 
With such a heart, even while being pressured by the times, he lived for the future and the world, which allowed him to ideologically unify the Chinese continent beyond the Warring States period. Not only that, but he also paved a way that could be left for all humanity beyond Asia. His desire to give what he could and his longing to share the truth ultimately shaped his character. From there, the teachings of Confucius emerged.

Father, please bless this time of holding the 6th National Holy Students Assembly, and through this opportunity, may the hearts of these young people, filled with passion, yearn for heaven and the universe, and may this be revealed in every page and every sentence of the books they read from now on.

May they become aware that they are representatives of the whole world and grow up with the solemn task of becoming heirs who will represent all humanity and the entire heaven. 

In this position, may they walk the doctrines of the Unification Church with a pure heart that others do not know. When they go to their villages, may they lay the groundwork for the world, and when they go to school, may they be able to advance with such convictions.

May they be the absolute key figures in expanding the heavenly realm, Father, and bless them to be able to make new resolutions and commitments with such hearts. 

Today, at this time, I thank you for allowing me to meet your beloved children and share a short time together, and through your words, may we have a time to gain new awareness and new resolutions. May we become sons and daughters who run to dedicate our lives before you, receiving praise and blessings from you. Thus, may we become owners who have no shame in being presented before all people. I earnestly ask for this, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
We must truly understand that You are our Father. 
Father, who is the center of the universe and the source of life, no matter how high and great Your infinite love, mercy, and compassion may be, we know that when we fail to face the true appearance of Your children, even that high and precious value cannot be manifested throughout this entire world. When we think that one appearance that can reveal Your precious value must have been the human ancestors in the Garden of Eden, we must once again pursue that position and, before hoping for tomorrow's heaven, we must long for You in our hearts and be able to appear in the likeness of You. The issue is how to complete such a self.

August 23, 1970 (Sunday), Central Training Center. 
* This message was given during the 6th National Holy Students Assembly.

We know this. 
Because humanity's ancestors fell and lost their original center and foundation, although originally humans had a relationship that should not be separated from You, due to the miserable historical path, we have come to have an unfortunate relationship that cannot be separated even if we wanted to. However, You have not abandoned such humans, and rather, the more we stand in opposition to You, wanting to betray You and separate from You, the more You have been working behind the scenes with a doubled heart, which the people on this earth did not know, nor did our ancestors know for sure.

The historical misfortune that has not escaped the ties of death still remains among our circumstances today, and when we think that we, who are connected with all the conditions and relationships of that reality, have not yet escaped from the realm of death, we must realize that Your laboring hand must be applied to us once again. In this desperate situation, we cannot suppress the shame of being children who bow our heads before You, who have worked from the past until now. However, when we have such a heart and come to feel Your heart, we earnestly hope and desire to be allowed to realize once again that You can connect with us from that position.

Those who follow Your path or believe in religion do not go with joy and laughter. When we think about the fact that we can only hold onto God in such a state of being a dropout in a miserable environment, where we can only meet tears, or in a crossroads where we are confused, we come to know that the place where we meet You is not a joyful reunion but a place of increasing misery and wretchedness, an indescribably pitiful place. We must understand how pitiful and miserable You are in dealing with such humanity and with ourselves.

When we think about how You have found Yourself in such a position, it is not because You have done something wrong. It is simply because humanity's ancestors made a mistake and put on the mask of sin, and we were born as descendants who could not take it off. However, You have walked the path of tears to save us, Your descendants, and to grant us a world of joy. We must understand that to prepare a foundation of happiness, we cannot escape from the sorrowful circumstances of Your relationship.

Now we must become true children who can call You our true Father. We must realize that You are not only the Lord who created the created world but also our Father. We must seek a Father who can be felt with all our cells and all our sensory organs, not an abstract Father.

Great Father, dignified Father, noble Father, who is the source of life and holds all authority over life and death, we must live with You. Since we were born because of You, we must have a firm belief and awareness that we must dedicate our lives to You. We earnestly hope and desire that You allow us to realize this clearly.

Your young children, scattered throughout South Korea, have gathered here. Who will guarantee their future? These are young boys and girls who cannot even promise themselves their own positions, so please take charge of them. Just as flowers bloom in the spring garden and their fragrance leads them to seek flowers unknowingly, may You move their original hearts so that they cannot help but be drawn to You and lead them to the free spring garden where they can embrace You. Thus, we earnestly hope and desire that they can experience infinite value and dwell in Your heart world, where they can boast of infinite value.

Please remember the positions of children whose circumstances are not free due to various reasons. Now, when we think that these children will grow to be the pillars of this nation in the next 10 or 20 years, we earnestly hope and desire that they realize how precious it is to grow up with a holy heart that longs for You, thinks of their country, thinks of the world, and loves humanity from their childhood.

Please be with the children of Yours who are attending this 6th National Holy Students Assembly and let them return with an unforgettable connection to You through this opportunity. We hope that we, who are in unfavorable circumstances, do not simply rejoice at seeing good environments but rather realize that there are tens of millions of nations that are more miserable and pitiful than us and that the world’s humanity remains. Let us first bear the trials they must face and stand in the position of a trial to bear the cross they must carry.

We earnestly hope and desire that You allow this time to be one where You are present and establish a relationship with these children regarding the future heaven You desire, and solidify the fate of this nation together with them.

Moreover, today is the Sabbath. I know that Your children scattered throughout South Korea are kneeling and bowing their heads, praying before You, longing for this place. Please bless them and embrace them with Your love.

Let them feel Your infinite mercy and allow them to feel the strength and pride of being those who can understand Your heart. Thus, we earnestly hope that they can become victors who can forget everything, endure everything, and overcome everything.

Father, please remember Your lonely children scattered throughout the world. Please be with the children who are busy preparing for the upcoming 700 couples' joint wedding ceremony. We earnestly ask and desire that You protect us so that all the things we are working on this year can align with Your providential will and we can pledge victory.

We earnestly ask that You bless Your children who are present here this morning, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> What did I write here? "I wrote 'New Sprout'." That's right. You are all teenagers, new sprouts. So today, I will talk about the title 'New Sprout.'

You are the new sprouts of the Republic of Korea. 
Since you are young people, you must aspire to become the owners of a nation in the future. Centered around the Republic of Korea, you must grow up as a new sprout to become the future's owners.

When you go to the mountains, you can see various types of trees. Even among the pines, you can see many different shapes. Some trees lean to the east, while others lean to the west, some to the south, and some to the north. There are also twisted trees, and there are tall, straight trees that look so majestic that anyone who sees them would say they are truly ideal trees.

When you go up to places like Namsan, you can see that the trees have not grown well, perhaps because the land is not good. The pines there are not straight but are crooked. However, if you go deep into the valleys of Gangwon-do, you will see trees that grow tall and straight. This is because the fallen leaves from the trees that have flourished through the seasons have accumulated and become natural fertilizer, and seeds have fallen into such soil, taking root and sprouting anew. We can see the shapes of such trees when we go up the mountain. Likewise, your appearances today must be similar to that.

So how do good trees grow well? In any region, there must be good land. Trees that grow in such places grow particularly well. However, no matter how good the land is, if the seed of that tree is not good, it will not thrive. If the tree is a crooked tree, it will surely resemble its ancestors.

Similarly, when we look at each of us today, we see that we have a variety of appearances, just like the trees that make up a garden. Just as there are various types of grass among the grass, we humans also have such appearances.

You know what kind of existence you are. You can compare your parents and siblings with others' parents and siblings to understand. You can also infer what kind of history your family has gone through. When you compare yourself with your younger siblings, if your younger sibling is better, then the family can develop, but if there are many younger siblings who are neither good-looking nor have a good character or future, then that family will decline.

Since you were born as descendants of ancestors with diverse appearances, you must have a connection with your ancestors. If we compare this to a seed, if the seed is a pine seed, it may look similar, but the value of that seed depends on the state of the original tree.

The seed is a summary of all the content that the tree has grown through until now. The future issues will be determined by how much value this seed has and whether it has the hope to be a seed that can develop infinitely in the future.

The next issue is the soil. No matter how good the seed is, if it falls on a stony field, it cannot become a being that can bear great fruit. Even if that seed sprouts, it does not know how many paths of suffering it must go through to grow into a tree. However, that seed cannot simply move to another place because the place it was born is not good. Even in a place where the decision of fate has been made, no matter how good the seed is, it is difficult for it to grow into a good tree.

However, if someone were to take that tree and transplant it into good soil and nurture it, that tree could grow well in good conditions along with its nature. Just as a seed sprouts from a seed, you are the new sprouts of the Republic of Korea. You are the new sprouts that this nation hopes for.

What must you do to become true sprouts? The national character of the Republic of Korea becomes the issue. Depending on the national character of the people of the Republic of Korea, it will determine what kind of sprouts you will become. You cannot escape the essence that your original ancestors possessed. You are at the first stage of being able to restart by concentrating all the essence of your ancestors, so you can be seen as the fate of the Republic of Korea.

When you have gone through historical eras and appeared as new sprouts as a result of the times, the question is what kind of historical significance the Republic of Korea possesses. Among the many countries in the world today, can the Republic of Korea become a tree that bears good fruit? The issue lies here. If it has become a good tree, it will bear good fruit. In other words, if that tree has grown in a better place than any other tree in the world, it will be able to obtain a seed that is better than any other seed through that tree. The issue is obtaining that seed.

After obtaining this seed, what must be done? It must be replanted. How should it be planted? If the planted tree is in good soil, it should not be moved elsewhere. If that place is truly good soil with no faults, then the seed should be sown in that land, right? However, if the seed is good but the environment is not suitable, what should be done? It must be transplanted. If that tree cannot be transplanted, it becomes an unfortunate tree. No matter how good the seed is from a good tree, if it is planted in bad soil, it cannot produce the second-best good seed that is desired.

From this perspective, if the Republic of Korea has been a good tree since the past and has received that seed to be planted in good soil, there would be no problem. However, if the tree is good but the environment is not suitable for the tree, what should be done? The tree must be transplanted. Who will transplant it? It cannot do it by itself. A third party must do it.

God desires good fruit.
So if God comes to save the world, what will He desire? He will desire good fruit. What will He do with the good fruit? He will plant that fruit in suitable good soil to create the materials that God needs most, which cannot be found anywhere else, to fulfill His purpose. Because of this desire, God has been seeking true sons until now.

Among the many nations of this world, there may be countries with good seeds but poor environments, and there may be countries with good environments but poor seeds. History is the same. If the entire world had good seeds, there would be no problem. If the world had grown from good seeds obtained from good trees, today this world would undoubtedly have become a world of peace, a world of hope, and a world with a guaranteed future.

However, the world we live in is not a world of peace, a world of hope, or a world where the future can be guaranteed; it has become a world where good and evil are intertwined. The surrounding environments have become more evil than good. Because the surroundings are surrounded by evil environments, no matter how good the seed is, it cannot bring about good results.

If God exists, He would not wish for that; if there are good seeds in an evil environment, how can good environments be created before those good seeds? If both the seed and the environment are evil, there is no hope.
You must completely eliminate it without any need to cry. When both the seed and the environment are bad, what would you do? Do you think there is any hope in that? When both the seed and the environment are bad, it must be burned away. It must be pulled out. Similarly, when both the seed and the environment are bad, God will also cut it off.

When looking at a person, whether that person has a good or bad seed is related to their foundation. If a person's seed is bad, it comes from a bad foundation. It is impossible to connect something that started from a bad foundation with something good. If the starting point is bad, the result cannot be good. If a human is made from bad seed, it is impossible to make that foundation good.

**Criteria for Determining Good and Evil**

In today’s evil environment, when we look at morality that pursues the values of mind, emotion, and will centered on our conscience, where do we set the standard? It is not set in the environment, but in the foundation of our original mind. The more you delve into the human heart's foundation, the cleaner it becomes. If that foundation is evil, shouldn’t it get worse the closer you get to the root? However, the more you delve into that foundation, the better the root is. When you see this, you can conclude that humans originally started from goodness. Isn’t that right?

Humans are originally good. They started from goodness. That is why we can also look at the standard of perfection of character; if it had started from evil, that would be impossible. When viewed this way, our human seed is not originally a bad seed. Do you understand?

Then, if the original seed is not a bad seed, why has it become a bad seed? There are numerous seeds, numerous people. When you look at your ancestors, if the right side is called good and the left side is called evil, there are many who have lived evilly like those on the left. There are many twists and turns. Good people have no twists and turns. This is different. If you look closely, you will find that you correspond to one of these categories. Do you understand?

Historically, when you see a good person, their ancestors were people who worked hard to seek goodness in public matters. In other words, those who seek truth and goodness are descendants of ancestors who were close to goodness. Isn’t that so? If one’s ancestors have many standards for pursuing goodness, then that standard shines through. Such people are close to goodness, so with just a little effort, they can enter a good place. However, if one’s ancestors were in a bad position through history, then they will become bad descendants. From that perspective, how difficult would it be to seek goodness?

So, what is the criterion for determining good and evil? You must clearly understand that it is determined by whether it is public or private. Even if we take the example of saying, “That friend is a good friend,” a good friend is someone who, when I call them a good friend, can also call me a good friend. If not, and if I think, “Oh, that guy is troublesome,” then they cannot be a good friend. Therefore, to find a good friend, you must overcome a hurdle. You must pioneer. To pioneer, what must you do? You must sweat, right? You must put in effort, right? Is it pioneering to just fly around in an airplane and look around? No, it is not. To pioneer, you must pay the price of effort that corresponds to it. That is why there is sweat and tears.

What determines whether your ancestors were good or evil? It is determined by whether your ancestors lived for themselves, for the country, or for the world. Living for one’s family is more public than living for oneself. So, who is the head of the family? It is the parents. That is why you must be filial to your parents. Do you understand? How do you show filial piety to your parents? Can you do it your own way? No, you cannot. Then, whose way must you follow? You must follow your parents' way. Because the public center of the family is the parents, you must follow their way. Following your parents' way means becoming one with their heart.

Parents hope that their children will inherit the public heavenly principles they have received from their ancestors and bear better fruits of value. That is why there are no parents who wish for their children to be worse off. Are there parents like that? No, there are not. No matter how much they are criminals or evil parents condemned by the world, they still seriously advise their children to do well.

When we look at this, the reason parents wish for their children to do better is that they are asking for their own salvation. Although the parents themselves have done many bad things, they are asking their children to save them. Throughout human history, regardless of the era, thoughtful or ambitious people have left behind their legacies, saying, “You must carry on this purpose and fulfill the responsibilities I could not complete.” 

The family is more public than the individual. Isn’t that right? Then, when we look at the family and lineage, which is more public? Living for the lineage is more public. The lineage has its leaders. The family must comply with the example of the lineage’s elders and become a model family that can stand in a senior position in the future. Being one with the person responsible for the lineage is more public than being one centered on the family.

**Why We Must Live Publicly**

So, why must we live publicly? What happens when we live publicly? No matter how many children a parent has, if there is one son who can completely accept and practice the parent's will one hundred percent, then everything the parent has belongs to that son. Is that true or not? Isn’t it so? Parents want to pass on everything they have to such a son. A son who can be loved is such a son.

If there is a neighborhood, the person who is most dedicated and loyal to that neighborhood will definitely become its leader. Is that true or not? That is how it is. If there is a Kim clan, and there is a family like that in the Kim clan, when the representative of that family influences the neighborhood, the leader of the Kim clan can take on the blessings of the neighborhood and become the village chief. Furthermore, when they unite with the county chief and live a more public life for the county, if that county chief is a person of purpose, to whom will they pass that position? They will pass it to someone who lives exemplary in a public position for the county.

If there is a country, living for the country is more public than living for the county. That is why we must fight for the country rather than for the county. We must prioritize the country. It is good to prioritize one’s parents, one’s neighborhood, one’s village, one’s county, and one’s province, but we must prioritize the country. The country includes the province, the county, the village, and the neighborhood. Therefore, when one becomes a complete public heir before their parents and has been loyal for the country, they become a person in a public position for the country and at the same time a true public person for the province, county, and village. That is why we are told to live for the highest public position. That is difficult.

To reach that position, how should one proceed? One cannot sit in the position of the president of the country just because they were filial to their parents. To do so, one must develop from the family to the neighborhood, village, county, and province, and then to the national level.

The factors that can determine goodness also include who has lived more publicly. So, what is public life? It is living for one’s parents, for the neighborhood, for the village, for the county, for the province, and for the country.

**Loyalty Centered on Humanity and Loyalty Centered on God**

A person who stands in a public position is called a loyal subject. A loyal subject must serve the people of the country, the county, the village, and the neighborhood. Why? Because the country continues to be a good country due to such central figures.

In the history of humanity, among the many countries, the question is which country has the most loyal subjects in the eyes of God. The loyal subjects referred to here are those who possess content that can align with God’s will, more than those centered on humanity. Do you understand what this means? The ranks of loyal subjects recognized by God differ from those recognized by the world. The path of loyal subjects seeking to establish the kingdom of heaven is different from the path of loyal subjects serving the country in the world. Why? Because this world is evil, and it is gradually going against the current to seek the country, while God has already prepared the kingdom and is coming forth. Thus, there are these two paths. When viewed this way, human history is a history of wars, which is also the history of the rise and fall of nations.

So, why do we fail to establish the tradition of loyal subjects recognized by God in that country? This is the problem. Why do we fail? It is because we have not completely aligned with the public position. If we had aligned, we would not fail. Can goodness fail? A country that is not good is destined to fail. This is the history of the rise and fall of nations. That is why God is leading us to a world of one purpose.

To support such mainstream thought, God is pursuing new individuals of goodness, families of goodness, tribes of goodness, nations of goodness, and a world of goodness. To achieve this world of goodness, He sends the center of goodness that can lead this evil world, and that person is the Messiah. The historical process that has supported His thought is religion. Do you understand? Yes. That is why it is valid to say that religion began before history.

Thus, the purpose of pursuing goodness centered on humanity and the purpose of pursuing goodness centered on God are different. This is another point: humanity cannot return to the world of goodness, and this is another point: that seed cannot become a perfect seed. Such a seed is a seed that has encountered an accident.

That is why there is forgiveness in God’s love. When forgiveness is given, this world cannot help but submit to God’s will. This may be somewhat distant from the term “sprout,” but when analyzing history, it is so.

**To Become a Pure Breed, You Must Obey**

You must now become a new seed. So, what kind of seed is that new seed? Is it just a seed that inherits the spirit of the patriots of the Republic of Korea? No, it is not enough. In this world, there are hybrids and pure breeds. To become a pure breed, you must obey. However, if you meet a bad master and obey, what will happen? You will become a bad seed. But if you meet a good master and obey, what will happen? You will become a good seed.

In this world, there are two masters. One is a fake, a fraud, a thief, and the other is the true one, a prince of the kingdom of heaven who comes as a scout. When you look at merchants, some have their stalls lined up, while others have just a few pieces of bread. When buying goods, there are people who flock to the advertisements, while there are also those who quietly look for good goods like scouts. Such things are happening in the world.

You must understand that there are two paths: the path of religion and the path of the world. So, who becomes the master on the path of religion? Can Satan be the master? No, he cannot. That is why religious people do not claim to be good. Is there anyone in the world who says, “Oh, let’s become good with a holy glass of whiskey”? Is there goodness in drinking and partying? Have you ever seen a literary novel that says, “At the end of this bottle lies goodness and happiness”? If you have seen it, that is a blatant lie. Have you ever seen a prosperous history in a country that indulges in drinking, dancing, and living lavishly? Have you heard of such an educational method? No, you have not. It is absolutely impossible. You are being told not to go that way at all.

You know how there are signs saying “No entry for minors” at places like theaters? Yet, do you want to go there or not? You want to go, right? That is strange. The fact that you want to go to a place that says not to go indicates that there is a problem with you. But do you have the confidence to prove that what you choose is definitely good? If so, then go. Can you confidently say, “I went where I wanted to go, and it was definitely good. Because I went because I liked it, I will never be sad or regret it”? If you can say that, then go. Do you have that confidence? You probably do not. That is why you are a patchwork of various influences.

Sometimes you feel pity for a poor person, and at other times you find it bothersome. You might think, “When I become president, I will have to cut off all their heads.” However, when it is your uncle or your sister or brother who is in that situation, you end up feeling pity for them. This shows how your thoughts change.

God is sending the most representative figure who can receive sympathy from humanity to us. In doing so, He establishes an emotional connection that cannot be severed.

The closest person to you is your parent. But when a parent suddenly passes away, who becomes the closest person? The servant who worked in your house becomes the closest person. Do you understand? No matter how much your parents lived well in the neighborhood, when they pass away and the family falls apart, that servant becomes like a parent.

In the same way, today, humanity is in a position of having lost their parents, so who does God send? He sends a servant. Then, for whom does that servant live their life? They live for the master's children. However, when the master's children are foolish, they do not recognize the servant’s good efforts. But when they mature and understand everything, they come to appreciate the servant who worked hard for them. It is the responsibility of the master's children, who have grown up under the servant's care, to lead the servant into a good environment. Isn’t that so?

In the same way, the history of restoration unfolds. Because humanity has fallen and is in an evil environment, God sent a servant to save them, but humanity did not recognize it and drove out all the heavenly servants. After driving them out, they still find that person in the world.
The realization that we were close to each other. After driving that person away, we come to know that person was the truest human among humans. This is how religion connects to the history of restoration. 
God is the highest public subject.
Until now, all religious leaders have walked a miserable path. It is important to understand that they did not walk this path for themselves, but for the people who follow them, their nations, and the world. In this way, they create a history that evokes emotional connections to a new world. To whom do we connect this? Not to an evil god, but to the true God. Therefore, the path centered on the true God must be public. 
What is this public nature? It is to serve something greater. The family is greater than the individual, the tribe is greater than the family, the nation is greater than the tribe, and the world is greater than the nation. Therefore, originally, religion started as a global religion, not as an ethnic religion. Thus, ethnic religions cannot exist. Ethnic religions will perish when the era of ethnic identities passes. Look at Christianity today. How did Christianity become a global religion? It is because the ideology of Christianity is a global ideology that can bind heaven and earth. 
Then, what is more public than this global aspect? It is God. 
Why? Because God is the highest public subject. Therefore, what is the highest teaching regarding humans? It is to become a person who dedicates their life and sincerity to God, rather than doing public work for the world. Such a person is the highest. That is why the Bible says, “You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind. This is the great and first commandment.” (Matthew 22:37-38) 
Why is that? When there is no king, one must love the nation in place of the king, but when the king is present, if one loves only the king, the nation will naturally come into their embrace even if they do not love it. Similarly, for a person who views the world as a public stage, the world is like the land. The world is like the land, but without a king, if one loves only the king, then both the king and the land become theirs. 
Then who is God? He is the master of the universe. Therefore, when one loves God, whose world does this become? It becomes the world of the person who loves God. That is why a religion that teaches based on the highest public standard can guide the world. Such a religion will remain until the end. This is precisely Christianity. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
If there is a child born into a wealthy family with a vast farm, does that child’s parents love them just because they ride horses every day? No, that is not the case. The parents love the child who helps them when they are struggling, even if the child does nothing at home and just idles around. Such a person is wise. This is akin to the positions of Esau and Jacob. 
The issue is God’s love. There is nothing more public than God’s love. Do you understand? What is the highest public aspect for humans? “God’s love.” Therefore, when one approaches the nation with God’s love, the nation is drawn to them; when one approaches friends with that love, friends are drawn to them; and when one approaches the world with that love, the world is conquered. 
To become the subject of love
When we look at young men and women, the girls often squint one eye and look at handsome men passing by, right? (Laughter) And even the less attractive men sneak glances at women, right? But suppose there is a man who appears dark and unattractive, like a catfish, and even when he wakes up, he has no charm. However, when viewed as a whole, he is manly. Such a man does not speak softly like women. He prioritizes action over words. Women might find this unpleasant. A man should say something first and then act, but this man charges in without any prelude. 
Initially, this might feel unpleasant, but if such a person can maintain that strong and wild character over time, women will reconsider. They might think, “Other men are deceitful and will fall away like leaves in autumn, and in winter they will wither. But this man, though a bit rustic, will push through like a piston under pressure; he will keep pushing until the end. He will be like that until he dies.” This changes a woman’s perception. Do you understand? 
Then, she will love the man as if he were the sky. When a strong love can emerge from that rough exterior, she will be drawn to him. Women should be cautious about this. (Laughter) Such scenarios are common in movies or novels, right? 
In the end, sincerity is the most important thing. Therefore, when emotional love is expressed, nothing can resist it. You might wonder if the teacher’s words are true, but they are. However, one should not say, “There is a beauty in my neighborhood’s school, so I will charge at her with sincerity.” (Laughter) Sincerity centered on oneself will not work. There must be a standard like “Let’s love our nation” that looks at more valuable content. 
Humans must not forget the thought of “Let’s love our nation. Let’s love heaven. Heaven and earth are mine.” This must always be in mind. When one centers on God or the world and says, “Let’s become one,” it will be, “Good. Let’s become one,” and they will love each other, leading the world to come into their embrace. According to the principles of our Unification Church, when plus and minus completely exchange, and that love ignites globally, God will be conquered by us. This is the formula. 
For that love to arise, where must it come from? It cannot come from the love motivated by oneself. Do you understand? Who is the protagonist of love? God. Yet men and women often talk about how their beloved is or how their love is. Is that the concept of love? 
Can you love alone? No matter how beautiful a person is, if there is no suitable partner, what good is it? It is worse than having none. Love is not something done alone.
