Have you experienced the personal spring season? If you have not experienced it, has that sprout attached to your personal roots? "Yes." Then, you must have become a blessed family, right? Have you attached to the family new sprout era? "No, I have not."

Become a tree that can cover the world.

The personal root is the root at the very bottom. Then the family rises, and then the tribe rises until it reaches the national standard. When that day comes... it means we have risen a lot.

So, where have you attached? "At the very bottom." If you have attached there, will you become a root or a sprout? What will you become? You must become a root for the individual and a sprout for the nation. That is the time we are in.

You must become a sprout of love. Where does that sprout come from? Among the roots, there is a central root, right? Doesn’t the tree grow from there? Isn’t that right? Now is that time.

This time will also come for you. So, what must you do? You must absorb all the nutrients that pass through the roots. In other words, you must become a root-like root that gives and receives well. In that position, the sprout will surely grow well.

Then, who is the center of the sprout? When we look at it centered on the Unification Church, who is the center of the sprout? "The teacher." It is the teacher, right? "Yes." How united are we centered on the teacher? We must have the strength to absorb nutrients and connect with the new sprouts while taking root in the Korean Peninsula. Only then can the sprouts grow. Is that right? "Yes." Do you have the strength to absorb nutrients and pass them on to the sprouts, or are you in a position of being dragged along? That is the question.

In that sense, if the teacher is the sprout, you must either become fertilizer, or if you cannot be fertilizer, you must become roots that can absorb nutrients, or you must become a sprout that can lead the roots. You must become one of these three. If you do not become one of the three, you have no relation to this tree. Those who have no relation are not on God's side but on Satan's side. The side of Satan goes to hell.

You are connected through God's love, which can connect all of this. You must know that and be planted in good soil with a true heart. Until now, the teacher has only extended roots and has not yet emerged as a sprout. He has only extended roots to survive the cold winter and to welcome spring. From now on, you must become the sprouts of the Unification Church. Otherwise, to restore the nation, you must either become roots or fertilizer. You must go out from that position.

That is why what we need most as sprouts is to draw closer to God. Only then will God protect you. When you go into that environment and align the sprouts and roots completely, you will know that you can become a great tree that can expand to the nation and even the world, covering the world. I hope you come to this gathering and resolve to become new sprouts or new roots. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Father! We have learned that you have led humanity by revealing the secrets of the spirit world through the parable of a tree in the Bible.
Father, we must become your true seeds, grow into true trees, bloom flowers, and bear fruit, manifesting as hundreds of seeds that can return to your embrace. Therefore, as we welcome the spring, please plant us as true seeds and allow us to grow as true trees in the land of freedom, so that we may be a comfort to you. Also, may we bear fruit in the fragrance of the flowers that emanate from there, fulfilling your desire to bring joy to the end times by sharing abundance with all nations.

Father, we thank you for allowing your young children to gather here. Please enable us to truly love you. We understand well that our past disobedience towards you was due to growing up in a wicked environment.

Father, amidst an environment filled with hope, centered on your public love, we must take root as a single seed in true soil, allowing our sprouts to grow in accordance with the law of a tree growing from its roots. We must recognize the importance of this environment that requires new sprouts.

Father, please beautify the youth era. Protect the paths of those connected to you, allowing them to grow based on the foundation of that environment. Make them true sprouts so that they can become trees of new life that all humanity can look upon and embrace, blooming new flowers and bearing fruit, so that we may be allowed to spread and remain in all nations.

We are pursuing a path of good history, but we lament that we have not had such a time centered on you. The more we look at the harsh realities of the evil world and the trials that come upon us, the more we understand how perilous the path of struggle we must take is. The harsher the environment, the more we must steadily gather ourselves, not being absorbed by the rushing evil environment, but rather becoming seeds and sprouts with self-control and subjectivity, possessing good vitality, and resolving to be a holy foundation that can lead us toward a new teacher, having not inherited this through our lifetime or the long historical process.

To do so, we must be strong. Father, allow this nation to be eternally united centered on your public love, a bond that cannot be severed by any force, nor changed by any adversity.

To endure such trials, we must supplement ourselves with sufficient nutrients. Guide us to become sons and daughters with the vitality to eliminate all conditions of evil remaining in this nation.

We earnestly hope and wish that we can appear before this nation as your sons and daughters, blessed to be welcomed as a nation of hope that the world desires.

Please pour out the gifts you wish to give abundantly upon this granted period. Thus, allow the boys and girls to create a new history in their homes or neighborhoods, in such environments.

Father, we know that when King Saul made mistakes, you grieved for him and anointed the young David to be king instead. We also know that David, who subdued Goliath, was faithful before God, and above all, his heart of faith in God was absolute, which is why you chose him as king. Likewise, we must also be strong and courageous. No matter what trials come, we must be strong and courageous. Our faith in you must be rock-solid.

Centered on your vitality and your realm of influence, may we grow as new sprouts that can absorb and explode the grievances of the nation and the world. We earnestly request that we become ourselves, possessing such strong power.

May you oversee the whole. We earnestly ask that you protect us until the remaining time, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
